Purpose:

This file contains a packed representation of the entire repository's contents.
It is designed to be easily consumable by AI systems for analysis, code review,
or other automated processes.

File Format:

The content is organized as follows:
1. This summary section

3. Directory structure
4. Repository files (if enabled)
5. Multiple file entries, each consisting of:
  a. A separator line (================)
  b. The file path (File: path/to/file)
  c. Another separator line
  d. The full contents of the file
  e. A blank line

Usage Guidelines:
-----------------
- This file should be treated as read-only. Any changes should be made to the
  original repository files, not this packed version.
- When processing this file, use the file path to distinguish
  between different files in the repository.
- Be aware that this file may contain sensitive information. Handle it with

 33:   function sanitizeValue(value, depth) {
 34:     if (depth === void 0) depth = 0;
 35:     if (depth > 5) return "[Max Depth]";
 36:     if (value === null) return null;
 37:     if (value === undefined) return undefined;
 38:     if (typeof value === "string") {
 39:       return value.length > 1000 ? value.slice(0, 1000) + "...[truncated]" : value;
 40:     }
 41:     if (typeof value !== "object") return value;
 42:     if (Array.isArray(value)) {
 43:       return value.slice(0, 100).map(function (v) {
 44:         return sanitizeValue(v, depth + 1);
 45:       });
 46:     }
 47:     var sanitized = {};
 48:     for (var k in value) {
 49:       if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(value, k)) {
 50:         var isSensitive = CONFIG.sensitiveFields.some(function (f) {
 51:           return k.toLowerCase().indexOf(f) !== -1;
 52:         });
 53:         if (isSensitive) {
 54:           sanitized[k] = "[REDACTED]";
 55:         } else {
 56:           sanitized[k] = sanitizeValue(value[k], depth + 1);
 57:         }
 58:       }
 59:     }
 60:     return sanitized;
 61:   }
 62:   function formatArg(arg) {
 63:     try {
 64:       if (arg instanceof Error) {
 65:         return { type: "Error", message: arg.message, stack: arg.stack };
 66:       }
 67:       if (typeof arg === "object") return sanitizeValue(arg);
 68:       return String(arg);
 69:     } catch (e) {
 70:       return "[Unserializable]";
 71:     }
 72:   }
 73:   function formatArgs(args) {
 74:     var result = [];
 75:     for (var i = 0; i < args.length; i++) result.push(formatArg(args[i]));
 76:     return result;
 77:   }
 78:   function pruneBuffer(buffer, maxSize) {
 79:     if (buffer.length > maxSize) buffer.splice(0, buffer.length - maxSize);
 80:   }
 81:   function tryParseJson(str) {
 82:     if (typeof str !== "string") return str;
 83:     try {
 84:       return JSON.parse(str);
 85:     } catch (e) {
 86:       return str;
 87:     }

 97:   function compactText(s, maxLen) {
 98:     try {
 99:       var t = (s || "").trim().replace(/\s+/g, " ");
100:       if (!t) return "";
101:       return t.length > maxLen ? t.slice(0, maxLen) + "…" : t;
102:     } catch (e) {
103:       return "";
104:     }
105:   }

114:   function describeElement(el) {
115:     if (!el || !(el instanceof Element)) return null;
116:     var getAttr = function (name) {
117:       return el.getAttribute(name);
118:     };
119:     var tag = el.tagName ? el.tagName.toLowerCase() : null;
120:     var id = el.id || null;
121:     var name = getAttr("name") || null;
122:     var role = getAttr("role") || null;
123:     var ariaLabel = getAttr("aria-label") || null;
124:     var dataLoc = getAttr("data-loc") || null;
125:     var testId =
126:       getAttr("data-testid") ||
127:       getAttr("data-test-id") ||
128:       getAttr("data-test") ||
129:       null;
130:     var type = tag === "input" ? (getAttr("type") || "text") : null;
131:     var href = tag === "a" ? getAttr("href") || null : null;
132:     var selectorHint = null;
133:     if (testId) selectorHint = '[data-testid="' + testId + '"]';
134:     else if (dataLoc) selectorHint = '[data-loc="' + dataLoc + '"]';
135:     else if (id) selectorHint = "#" + id;
136:     else selectorHint = tag || "unknown";
137:     return {
138:       tag: tag,
139:       id: id,
140:       name: name,
141:       type: type,
142:       role: role,
143:       ariaLabel: ariaLabel,
144:       testId: testId,
145:       dataLoc: dataLoc,
146:       href: href,
147:       text: elText(el),
148:       selectorHint: selectorHint,
149:     };
150:   }
151:   function isSensitiveField(el) {
152:     if (!el || !(el instanceof Element)) return false;
153:     var tag = el.tagName ? el.tagName.toLowerCase() : "";
154:     if (tag !== "input" && tag !== "textarea") return false;
155:     var type = (el.getAttribute("type") || "").toLowerCase();
156:     if (type === "password") return true;
157:     var name = (el.getAttribute("name") || "").toLowerCase();
158:     var id = (el.id || "").toLowerCase();
159:     return CONFIG.sensitiveFields.some(function (f) {
160:       return name.indexOf(f) !== -1 || id.indexOf(f) !== -1;
161:     });
162:   }
163:   function getInputValueSafe(el) {
164:     if (!el || !(el instanceof Element)) return null;
165:     var tag = el.tagName ? el.tagName.toLowerCase() : "";
166:     if (tag !== "input" && tag !== "textarea" && tag !== "select") return null;
167:     var v = "";
168:     try {
169:       v = el.value != null ? String(el.value) : "";
170:     } catch (e) {
171:       v = "";
172:     }

174:     if (v.length > CONFIG.uiInputMaxLen) v = v.slice(0, CONFIG.uiInputMaxLen) + "…";
175:     return v;
176:   }

354:   var originalFetch = window.fetch.bind(window);
355:   window.fetch = function (input, init) {
356:     init = init || {};
357:     var startTime = Date.now();
358:     var url = typeof input === "string"
359:       ? input
360:       : (input && (input.url || input.href || String(input))) || "";
361:     var method = init.method || (input && input.method) || "GET";
362:     if (url.indexOf("/__manus__/") === 0) {
363:       return originalFetch(input, init);
364:     }
365:     var requestHeaders = {};
366:     try {
367:       if (init.headers) {
368:         requestHeaders = Object.fromEntries(new Headers(init.headers).entries());
369:       }
370:     } catch (e) {
371:       requestHeaders = { _parseError: true };
372:     }
373:     var entry = {
374:       timestamp: startTime,
375:       type: "fetch",
376:       method: method.toUpperCase(),
377:       url: url,
378:       request: {
379:         headers: requestHeaders,
380:         body: init.body ? sanitizeValue(tryParseJson(init.body)) : null,
381:       },
382:       response: null,
383:       duration: null,
384:       error: null,
385:     };
386:     return originalFetch(input, init)
387:       .then(function (response) {
388:         entry.duration = Date.now() - startTime;
389:         var contentType = (response.headers.get("content-type") || "").toLowerCase();
390:         var contentLength = response.headers.get("content-length");
391:         entry.response = {
392:           status: response.status,
393:           statusText: response.statusText,
394:           headers: Object.fromEntries(response.headers.entries()),
395:           body: null,
396:         };
397:         if (response.status >= 400) {
398:           logUiEvent("network_error", {
399:             kind: "fetch",
400:             method: entry.method,
401:             url: entry.url,
402:             status: response.status,
403:             statusText: response.statusText,
404:           });
405:         }
406:         var isStreaming = contentType.indexOf("text/event-stream") !== -1 ||
407:                           contentType.indexOf("application/stream") !== -1 ||
408:                           contentType.indexOf("application/x-ndjson") !== -1;
409:         if (isStreaming) {
410:           entry.response.body = "[Streaming response - not captured]";
411:           store.networkRequests.push(entry);
412:           pruneBuffer(store.networkRequests, CONFIG.bufferSize.network);
413:           return response;
414:         }
415:         if (contentLength && parseInt(contentLength, 10) > CONFIG.maxBodyLength) {
416:           entry.response.body = "[Response too large: " + contentLength + " bytes]";
417:           store.networkRequests.push(entry);
418:           pruneBuffer(store.networkRequests, CONFIG.bufferSize.network);
419:           return response;
420:         }
421:         var isBinary = contentType.indexOf("image/") !== -1 ||
422:                        contentType.indexOf("video/") !== -1 ||
423:                        contentType.indexOf("audio/") !== -1 ||
424:                        contentType.indexOf("application/octet-stream") !== -1 ||
425:                        contentType.indexOf("application/pdf") !== -1 ||
426:                        contentType.indexOf("application/zip") !== -1;
427:         if (isBinary) {
428:           entry.response.body = "[Binary content: " + contentType + "]";
429:           store.networkRequests.push(entry);
430:           pruneBuffer(store.networkRequests, CONFIG.bufferSize.network);
431:           return response;
432:         }
433:         var clonedResponse = response.clone();
434:         clonedResponse
435:           .text()
436:           .then(function (text) {
437:             if (text.length <= CONFIG.maxBodyLength) {
438:               entry.response.body = sanitizeValue(tryParseJson(text));
439:             } else {
440:               entry.response.body = text.slice(0, CONFIG.maxBodyLength) + "...[truncated]";
441:             }
442:           })
443:           .catch(function () {
444:             entry.response.body = "[Unable to read body]";
445:           })
446:           .finally(function () {
447:             store.networkRequests.push(entry);
448:             pruneBuffer(store.networkRequests, CONFIG.bufferSize.network);
449:           });
450:         return response;
451:       })
452:       .catch(function (error) {
453:         entry.duration = Date.now() - startTime;
454:         entry.error = { message: error.message, stack: error.stack };
455:         store.networkRequests.push(entry);
456:         pruneBuffer(store.networkRequests, CONFIG.bufferSize.network);
457:         logUiEvent("network_error", {
458:           kind: "fetch",
459:           method: entry.method,
460:           url: entry.url,
461:           message: error.message,
462:         });
463:         throw error;
464:       });
465:   };
466:   var originalXHROpen = XMLHttpRequest.prototype.open;
467:   var originalXHRSend = XMLHttpRequest.prototype.send;
468:   XMLHttpRequest.prototype.open = function (method, url) {
469:     this._manusData = {
470:       method: (method || "GET").toUpperCase(),
471:       url: url,
472:       startTime: null,
473:     };
474:     return originalXHROpen.apply(this, arguments);

476:   XMLHttpRequest.prototype.send = function (body) {
477:     var xhr = this;
478:     if (
479:       xhr._manusData &&
480:       xhr._manusData.url &&
481:       xhr._manusData.url.indexOf("/__manus__/") !== 0
482:     ) {
483:       xhr._manusData.startTime = Date.now();
484:       xhr._manusData.requestBody = body ? sanitizeValue(tryParseJson(body)) : null;
485:       xhr.addEventListener("load", function () {
486:         var contentType = (xhr.getResponseHeader("content-type") || "").toLowerCase();
487:         var responseBody = null;
488:         // Skip body capture for streaming responses
489:         var isStreaming = contentType.indexOf("text/event-stream") !== -1 ||
490:                           contentType.indexOf("application/stream") !== -1 ||
491:                           contentType.indexOf("application/x-ndjson") !== -1;
492:         var isBinary = contentType.indexOf("image/") !== -1 ||
493:                        contentType.indexOf("video/") !== -1 ||
494:                        contentType.indexOf("audio/") !== -1 ||
495:                        contentType.indexOf("application/octet-stream") !== -1 ||
496:                        contentType.indexOf("application/pdf") !== -1 ||
497:                        contentType.indexOf("application/zip") !== -1;
498:         if (isStreaming) {
499:           responseBody = "[Streaming response - not captured]";
500:         } else if (isBinary) {
501:           responseBody = "[Binary content: " + contentType + "]";
502:         } else {
503:           try {
504:             var text = xhr.responseText || "";
505:             if (text.length > CONFIG.maxBodyLength) {
506:               responseBody = text.slice(0, CONFIG.maxBodyLength) + "...[truncated]";
507:             } else {
508:               responseBody = sanitizeValue(tryParseJson(text));
509:             }
510:           } catch (e) {
511:             // responseText may throw for non-text responses
512:             responseBody = "[Unable to read response: " + e.message + "]";
513:           }
514:         }
515:         var entry = {
516:           timestamp: xhr._manusData.startTime,
517:           type: "xhr",
518:           method: xhr._manusData.method,
519:           url: xhr._manusData.url,
520:           request: { body: xhr._manusData.requestBody },
521:           response: {
522:             status: xhr.status,
523:             statusText: xhr.statusText,
524:             body: responseBody,
525:           },
526:           duration: Date.now() - xhr._manusData.startTime,
527:           error: null,
528:         };
529:         store.networkRequests.push(entry);
530:         pruneBuffer(store.networkRequests, CONFIG.bufferSize.network);
531:         if (entry.response && entry.response.status >= 400) {
532:           logUiEvent("network_error", {
533:             kind: "xhr",
534:             method: entry.method,
535:             url: entry.url,
536:             status: entry.response.status,
537:             statusText: entry.response.statusText,
538:           });
539:         }
540:       });
541:       xhr.addEventListener("error", function () {
542:         var entry = {
543:           timestamp: xhr._manusData.startTime,
544:           type: "xhr",
545:           method: xhr._manusData.method,
546:           url: xhr._manusData.url,
547:           request: { body: xhr._manusData.requestBody },
548:           response: null,
549:           duration: Date.now() - xhr._manusData.startTime,
550:           error: { message: "Network error" },
551:         };
552:         store.networkRequests.push(entry);
553:         pruneBuffer(store.networkRequests, CONFIG.bufferSize.network);
554:         logUiEvent("network_error", {
555:           kind: "xhr",
556:           method: entry.method,
557:           url: entry.url,
558:           message: "Network error",
559:         });
560:       });
561:     }
562:     return originalXHRSend.apply(this, arguments);
563:   };
564:   function reportLogs() {
565:     var consoleLogs = store.consoleLogs.splice(0);
566:     var networkRequests = store.networkRequests.splice(0);
567:     var uiEvents = store.uiEvents.splice(0);
568:     if (
569:       consoleLogs.length === 0 &&
570:       networkRequests.length === 0 &&
571:       uiEvents.length === 0
572:     ) {
573:       return Promise.resolve();
574:     }
575:     var payload = {
576:       timestamp: Date.now(),
577:       consoleLogs: consoleLogs,
578:       networkRequests: networkRequests,
579:       sessionEvents: uiEvents,
580:       uiEvents: uiEvents,
581:     };
582:     return originalFetch(CONFIG.reportEndpoint, {
583:       method: "POST",
584:       headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
585:       body: JSON.stringify(payload),
586:     }).catch(function () {
587:       store.consoleLogs = consoleLogs.concat(store.consoleLogs);
588:       store.networkRequests = networkRequests.concat(store.networkRequests);
589:       store.uiEvents = uiEvents.concat(store.uiEvents);
590:       pruneBuffer(store.consoleLogs, CONFIG.bufferSize.console);
591:       pruneBuffer(store.networkRequests, CONFIG.bufferSize.network);
592:       pruneBuffer(store.uiEvents, CONFIG.bufferSize.ui);
593:     });
594:   }
595:   setInterval(reportLogs, CONFIG.reportInterval);
596:   window.addEventListener("beforeunload", function () {
597:     var consoleLogs = store.consoleLogs;
598:     var networkRequests = store.networkRequests;
599:     var uiEvents = store.uiEvents;
600:     if (
601:       consoleLogs.length === 0 &&
602:       networkRequests.length === 0 &&
603:       uiEvents.length === 0
604:     ) {
605:       return;
606:     }
607:     var payload = {
608:       timestamp: Date.now(),
609:       consoleLogs: consoleLogs,
610:       networkRequests: networkRequests,
611:       sessionEvents: uiEvents,
612:       uiEvents: uiEvents,
613:     };
614:     if (navigator.sendBeacon) {
615:       var payloadStr = JSON.stringify(payload);
616:       var MAX_BEACON_SIZE = 60000;
617:       if (payloadStr.length > MAX_BEACON_SIZE) {
618:         var truncatedPayload = {
619:           timestamp: Date.now(),
620:           consoleLogs: consoleLogs.slice(-50),
621:           networkRequests: networkRequests.slice(-20),
622:           sessionEvents: uiEvents.slice(-100),
623:           uiEvents: uiEvents.slice(-100),
624:           _truncated: true,
625:         };
626:         payloadStr = JSON.stringify(truncatedPayload);
627:       }
628:       navigator.sendBeacon(CONFIG.reportEndpoint, payloadStr);
629:     }
630:   });
631:   try {
632:     installUiEventListeners();
633:   } catch (e) {
634:     console.warn("[Manus] Failed to install UI listeners:", e);
635:   }
636:   window.__MANUS_DEBUG_COLLECTOR__ = {
637:     version: "2.0-no-rrweb",
638:     store: store,
639:     forceReport: reportLogs,
640:   };
641:   console.debug("[Manus] Debug collector initialized (no rrweb, UI events only)");
642: })();

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/client/src/_core/hooks/useAuth.ts
================
 1: import { getLoginUrl } from "@/const";
 2: import { trpc } from "@/lib/trpc";
 3: import { TRPCClientError } from "@trpc/client";
 4: import { useCallback, useEffect, useMemo } from "react";
 5: type UseAuthOptions = {
 6:   redirectOnUnauthenticated?: boolean;
 7:   redirectPath?: string;
 8: };
 9: export function useAuth(options?: UseAuthOptions) {
10:   const { redirectOnUnauthenticated = false, redirectPath = getLoginUrl() } =
11:     options ?? {};
12:   const utils = trpc.useUtils();
13:   const meQuery = trpc.auth.me.useQuery(undefined, {
14:     retry: false,
15:     refetchOnWindowFocus: false,
16:   });
17:   const logoutMutation = trpc.auth.logout.useMutation({
18:     onSuccess: () => {
19:       utils.auth.me.setData(undefined, null);
20:     },
21:   });
22:   const logout = useCallback(async () => {
23:     try {
24:       await logoutMutation.mutateAsync();
25:     } catch (error: unknown) {
26:       if (
27:         error instanceof TRPCClientError &&
28:         error.data?.code === "UNAUTHORIZED"
29:       ) {
30:         return;
31:       }
32:       throw error;
33:     } finally {
34:       utils.auth.me.setData(undefined, null);
35:       await utils.auth.me.invalidate();
36:     }
37:   }, [logoutMutation, utils]);
38:   const state = useMemo(() => {
39:     localStorage.setItem(
40:       "manus-runtime-user-info",
41:       JSON.stringify(meQuery.data)
42:     );
43:     return {
44:       user: meQuery.data ?? null,
45:       loading: meQuery.isLoading || logoutMutation.isPending,
46:       error: meQuery.error ?? logoutMutation.error ?? null,
47:       isAuthenticated: Boolean(meQuery.data),
48:     };
49:   }, [
50:     meQuery.data,
51:     meQuery.error,
52:     meQuery.isLoading,
53:     logoutMutation.error,
54:     logoutMutation.isPending,
55:   ]);
56:   useEffect(() => {
57:     if (!redirectOnUnauthenticated) return;
58:     if (meQuery.isLoading || logoutMutation.isPending) return;
59:     if (state.user) return;
60:     if (typeof window === "undefined") return;
61:     if (window.location.pathname === redirectPath) return;
62:     window.location.href = redirectPath
63:   }, [
64:     redirectOnUnauthenticated,
65:     redirectPath,
66:     logoutMutation.isPending,
67:     meQuery.isLoading,
68:     state.user,
69:   ]);
70:   return {
71:     ...state,
72:     refresh: () => meQuery.refetch(),
73:     logout,
74:   };
75: }

================
File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/client/src/components/ui/carousel.tsx
================
  1: import * as React from "react";
  2: import useEmblaCarousel, {
  3:   type UseEmblaCarouselType,
  4: } from "embla-carousel-react";
  5: import { ArrowLeft, ArrowRight } from "lucide-react";
  6: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
  7: import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
  8: type CarouselApi = UseEmblaCarouselType[1];
  9: type UseCarouselParameters = Parameters<typeof useEmblaCarousel>;
 10: type CarouselOptions = UseCarouselParameters[0];
 11: type CarouselPlugin = UseCarouselParameters[1];
 12: type CarouselProps = {
 13:   opts?: CarouselOptions;
 14:   plugins?: CarouselPlugin;
 15:   orientation?: "horizontal" | "vertical";
 16:   setApi?: (api: CarouselApi) => void;
 17: };
 18: type CarouselContextProps = {
 19:   carouselRef: ReturnType<typeof useEmblaCarousel>[0];
 20:   api: ReturnType<typeof useEmblaCarousel>[1];
 21:   scrollPrev: () => void;
 22:   scrollNext: () => void;
 23:   canScrollPrev: boolean;
 24:   canScrollNext: boolean;
 25: } & CarouselProps;
 26: const CarouselContext = React.createContext<CarouselContextProps | null>(null);
 27: function useCarousel() {
 28:   const context = React.useContext(CarouselContext);
 29:   if (!context) {
 30:     throw new Error("useCarousel must be used within a <Carousel />");
 31:   }
 32:   return context;
 33: }
 34: function Carousel({
 35:   orientation = "horizontal",
 36:   opts,
 37:   setApi,
 38:   plugins,
 39:   className,
 40:   children,
 41:   ...props
 42: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & CarouselProps) {
 43:   const [carouselRef, api] = useEmblaCarousel(
 44:     {
 45:       ...opts,
 46:       axis: orientation === "horizontal" ? "x" : "y",
 47:     },
 48:     plugins
 49:   );
 50:   const [canScrollPrev, setCanScrollPrev] = React.useState(false);
 51:   const [canScrollNext, setCanScrollNext] = React.useState(false);
 52:   const onSelect = React.useCallback((api: CarouselApi) => {
 53:     if (!api) return;
 54:     setCanScrollPrev(api.canScrollPrev());
 55:     setCanScrollNext(api.canScrollNext());
 56:   }, []);
 57:   const scrollPrev = React.useCallback(() => {
 58:     api?.scrollPrev();
 59:   }, [api]);
 60:   const scrollNext = React.useCallback(() => {
 61:     api?.scrollNext();
 62:   }, [api]);
 63:   const handleKeyDown = React.useCallback(
 64:     (event: React.KeyboardEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
 65:       if (event.key === "ArrowLeft") {
 66:         event.preventDefault();
 67:         scrollPrev();
 68:       } else if (event.key === "ArrowRight") {
 69:         event.preventDefault();
 70:         scrollNext();
 71:       }
 72:     },
 73:     [scrollPrev, scrollNext]
 74:   );
 75:   React.useEffect(() => {
 76:     if (!api || !setApi) return;
 77:     setApi(api);
 78:   }, [api, setApi]);
 79:   React.useEffect(() => {
 80:     if (!api) return;
 81:     onSelect(api);
 82:     api.on("reInit", onSelect);
 83:     api.on("select", onSelect);
 84:     return () => {
 85:       api?.off("select", onSelect);
 86:     };
 87:   }, [api, onSelect]);
 88:   return (
 89:     <CarouselContext.Provider
 90:       value={{
 91:         carouselRef,
 92:         api: api,
 93:         opts,
 94:         orientation:
 95:           orientation || (opts?.axis === "y" ? "vertical" : "horizontal"),
 96:         scrollPrev,
 97:         scrollNext,
 98:         canScrollPrev,
 99:         canScrollNext,
100:       }}
101:     >
102:       <div
103:         onKeyDownCapture={handleKeyDown}
104:         className={cn("relative", className)}
105:         role="region"
106:         aria-roledescription="carousel"
107:         data-slot="carousel"
108:         {...props}
109:       >
110:         {children}
111:       </div>
112:     </CarouselContext.Provider>
113:   );
114: }
115: function CarouselContent({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
116:   const { carouselRef, orientation } = useCarousel();
117:   return (
118:     <div
119:       ref={carouselRef}
120:       className="overflow-hidden"
121:       data-slot="carousel-content"
122:     >
123:       <div
124:         className={cn(
125:           "flex",
126:           orientation === "horizontal" ? "-ml-4" : "-mt-4 flex-col",
127:           className
128:         )}
129:         {...props}
130:       />
131:     </div>
132:   );
133: }
134: function CarouselItem({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
135:   const { orientation } = useCarousel();
136:   return (
137:     <div
138:       role="group"
139:       aria-roledescription="slide"
140:       data-slot="carousel-item"
141:       className={cn(
142:         "min-w-0 shrink-0 grow-0 basis-full",
143:         orientation === "horizontal" ? "pl-4" : "pt-4",
144:         className
145:       )}
146:       {...props}
147:     />
148:   );
149: }
150: function CarouselPrevious({
151:   className,
152:   variant = "outline",
153:   size = "icon",
154:   ...props
155: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof Button>) {
156:   const { orientation, scrollPrev, canScrollPrev } = useCarousel();
157:   return (
158:     <Button
159:       data-slot="carousel-previous"
160:       variant={variant}
161:       size={size}
162:       className={cn(
163:         "absolute size-8 rounded-full",
164:         orientation === "horizontal"
165:           ? "top-1/2 -left-12 -translate-y-1/2"
166:           : "-top-12 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 rotate-90",
167:         className
168:       )}
169:       disabled={!canScrollPrev}
170:       onClick={scrollPrev}
171:       {...props}
172:     >
173:       <ArrowLeft />
174:       <span className="sr-only">Previous slide</span>
175:     </Button>
176:   );
177: }
178: function CarouselNext({
179:   className,
180:   variant = "outline",
181:   size = "icon",
182:   ...props
183: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof Button>) {
184:   const { orientation, scrollNext, canScrollNext } = useCarousel();

196:       )}

  1: import * as React from "react";
  2: import * as RechartsPrimitive from "recharts";
  3: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
  4: const THEMES = { light: "", dark: ".dark" } as const;
  5: export type ChartConfig = {
  6:   [k in string]: {
  7:     label?: React.ReactNode;
  8:     icon?: React.ComponentType;
  9:   } & (
 10:     | { color?: string; theme?: never }
 11:     | { color?: never; theme: Record<keyof typeof THEMES, string> }
 12:   );
 13: };
 14: type ChartContextProps = {
 15:   config: ChartConfig;
 16: };
 17: const ChartContext = React.createContext<ChartContextProps | null>(null);
 18: function useChart() {
 19:   const context = React.useContext(ChartContext);
 20:   if (!context) {
 21:     throw new Error("useChart must be used within a <ChartContainer />");
 22:   }
 23:   return context;
 24: }
 25: function ChartContainer({
 26:   id,
 27:   className,
 28:   children,
 29:   config,
 30:   ...props
 31: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
 32:   config: ChartConfig;
 33:   children: React.ComponentProps<
 34:     typeof RechartsPrimitive.ResponsiveContainer
 35:   >["children"];
 36: }) {
 37:   const uniqueId = React.useId();
 38:   const chartId = `chart-${id || uniqueId.replace(/:/g, "")}`;
 39:   return (
 40:     <ChartContext.Provider value={{ config }}>
 41:       <div
 42:         data-slot="chart"
 43:         data-chart={chartId}
 44:         className={cn(
 45:           "[&_.recharts-cartesian-axis-tick_text]:fill-muted-foreground [&_.recharts-cartesian-grid_line[stroke='#ccc']]:stroke-border/50 [&_.recharts-curve.recharts-tooltip-cursor]:stroke-border [&_.recharts-polar-grid_[stroke='#ccc']]:stroke-border [&_.recharts-radial-bar-background-sector]:fill-muted [&_.recharts-rectangle.recharts-tooltip-cursor]:fill-muted [&_.recharts-reference-line_[stroke='#ccc']]:stroke-border flex aspect-video justify-center text-xs [&_.recharts-dot[stroke='#fff']]:stroke-transparent [&_.recharts-layer]:outline-hidden [&_.recharts-sector]:outline-hidden [&_.recharts-sector[stroke='#fff']]:stroke-transparent [&_.recharts-surface]:outline-hidden",
 46:           className
 47:         )}
 48:         {...props}
 49:       >
 50:         <ChartStyle id={chartId} config={config} />
 51:         <RechartsPrimitive.ResponsiveContainer>
 52:           {children}
 53:         </RechartsPrimitive.ResponsiveContainer>
 54:       </div>
 55:     </ChartContext.Provider>
 56:   );
 57: }
 58: const ChartStyle = ({ id, config }: { id: string; config: ChartConfig }) => {
 59:   const colorConfig = Object.entries(config).filter(
 60:     ([, config]) => config.theme || config.color
 61:   );
 62:   if (!colorConfig.length) {
 63:     return null;
 64:   }
 65:   return (
 66:     <style
 67:       dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{
 68:         __html: Object.entries(THEMES)
 69:           .map(
 70:             ([theme, prefix]) => `
 71: ${prefix} [data-chart=${id}] {
 72: ${colorConfig
 73:   .map(([key, itemConfig]) => {
 74:     const color =
 75:       itemConfig.theme?.[theme as keyof typeof itemConfig.theme] ||
 76:       itemConfig.color;
 77:     return color ? `  --color-${key}: ${color};` : null;
 78:   })
 79:   .join("\n")}
 80: }
 81: `
 82:           )
 83:           .join("\n"),
 84:       }}
 85:     />
 86:   );
 87: };
 88: const ChartTooltip = RechartsPrimitive.Tooltip;
 89: function ChartTooltipContent({
 90:   active,
 91:   payload,
 92:   className,
 93:   indicator = "dot",
 94:   hideLabel = false,
 95:   hideIndicator = false,
 96:   label,
 97:   labelFormatter,
 98:   labelClassName,
 99:   formatter,
100:   color,
101:   nameKey,
102:   labelKey,
103: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof RechartsPrimitive.Tooltip> &
104:   React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
105:     hideLabel?: boolean;
106:     hideIndicator?: boolean;
107:     indicator?: "line" | "dot" | "dashed";
108:     nameKey?: string;
109:     labelKey?: string;
110:   }) {
111:   const { config } = useChart();
112:   const tooltipLabel = React.useMemo(() => {
113:     if (hideLabel || !payload?.length) {
114:       return null;
115:     }
116:     const [item] = payload;
117:     const key = `${labelKey || item?.dataKey || item?.name || "value"}`;
118:     const itemConfig = getPayloadConfigFromPayload(config, item, key);
119:     const value =
120:       !labelKey && typeof label === "string"
121:         ? config[label as keyof typeof config]?.label || label
122:         : itemConfig?.label;
123:     if (labelFormatter) {
124:       return (
125:         <div className={cn("font-medium", labelClassName)}>
126:           {labelFormatter(value, payload)}
127:         </div>
128:       );
129:     }
130:     if (!value) {
131:       return null;
132:     }
133:     return <div className={cn("font-medium", labelClassName)}>{value}</div>;
134:   }, [
135:     label,
136:     labelFormatter,
137:     payload,
138:     hideLabel,
139:     labelClassName,
140:     config,
141:     labelKey,
142:   ]);
143:   if (!active || !payload?.length) {
144:     return null;
145:   }
146:   const nestLabel = payload.length === 1 && indicator !== "dot";
147:   return (
148:     <div
149:       className={cn(
150:         "border-border/50 bg-background grid min-w-[8rem] items-start gap-1.5 rounded-lg border px-2.5 py-1.5 text-xs shadow-xl",
151:         className
152:       )}
153:     >
154:       {!nestLabel ? tooltipLabel : null}
155:       <div className="grid gap-1.5">
156:         {payload
157:           .filter(item => item.type !== "none")
158:           .map((item, index) => {
159:             const key = `${nameKey || item.name || item.dataKey || "value"}`;
160:             const itemConfig = getPayloadConfigFromPayload(config, item, key);
161:             const indicatorColor = color || item.payload.fill || item.color;
162:             return (
163:               <div
164:                 key={item.dataKey}
165:                 className={cn(
166:                   "[&>svg]:text-muted-foreground flex w-full flex-wrap items-stretch gap-2 [&>svg]:h-2.5 [&>svg]:w-2.5",
167:                   indicator === "dot" && "items-center"
168:                 )}
169:               >
170:                 {formatter && item?.value !== undefined && item.name ? (
171:                   formatter(item.value, item.name, item, index, item.payload)
172:                 ) : (
173:                   <>
174:                     {itemConfig?.icon ? (
175:                       <itemConfig.icon />
176:                     ) : (
177:                       !hideIndicator && (
178:                         <div
179:                           className={cn(
180:                             "shrink-0 rounded-[2px] border-(--color-border) bg-(--color-bg)",
181:                             {
182:                               "h-2.5 w-2.5": indicator === "dot",
183:                               "w-1": indicator === "line",
184:                               "w-0 border-[1.5px] border-dashed bg-transparent":
185:                                 indicator === "dashed",
186:                               "my-0.5": nestLabel && indicator === "dashed",
187:                             }
188:                           )}
189:                           style={
190:                             {
191:                               "--color-bg": indicatorColor,
192:                               "--color-border": indicatorColor,
193:                             } as React.CSSProperties
194:                           }
195:                         />
196:                       )
197:                     )}
198:                     <div
199:                       className={cn(
200:                         "flex flex-1 justify-between leading-none",
201:                         nestLabel ? "items-end" : "items-center"
202:                       )}
203:                     >
204:                       <div className="grid gap-1.5">
205:                         {nestLabel ? tooltipLabel : null}
206:                         <span className="text-muted-foreground">
207:                           {itemConfig?.label || item.name}
208:                         </span>
209:                       </div>
210:                       {item.value && (
211:                         <span className="text-foreground font-mono font-medium tabular-nums">
212:                           {item.value.toLocaleString()}
213:                         </span>
214:                       )}
215:                     </div>
216:                   </>
217:                 )}
218:               </div>
219:             );
220:           })}
221:       </div>
222:     </div>
223:   );
224: }
225: const ChartLegend = RechartsPrimitive.Legend;
226: function ChartLegendContent({
227:   className,
228:   hideIcon = false,
229:   payload,
230:   verticalAlign = "bottom",
231:   nameKey,
232: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> &
233:   Pick<RechartsPrimitive.LegendProps, "payload" | "verticalAlign"> & {
234:     hideIcon?: boolean;
235:     nameKey?: string;
236:   }) {
237:   const { config } = useChart();
238:   if (!payload?.length) {
239:     return null;
240:   }
241:   return (
242:     <div
243:       className={cn(
244:         "flex items-center justify-center gap-4",
245:         verticalAlign === "top" ? "pb-3" : "pt-3",
246:         className
247:       )}
248:     >
249:       {payload
250:         .filter(item => item.type !== "none")
251:         .map(item => {
252:           const key = `${nameKey || item.dataKey || "value"}`;
253:           const itemConfig = getPayloadConfigFromPayload(config, item, key);
254:           return (
255:             <div
256:               key={item.value}
257:               className={cn(
258:                 "[&>svg]:text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-1.5 [&>svg]:h-3 [&>svg]:w-3"
259:               )}
260:             >
261:               {itemConfig?.icon && !hideIcon ? (
262:                 <itemConfig.icon />
263:               ) : (
264:                 <div
265:                   className="h-2 w-2 shrink-0 rounded-[2px]"
266:                   style={{
267:                     backgroundColor: item.color,
268:                   }}
269:                 />
270:               )}
271:               {itemConfig?.label}
272:             </div>
273:           );
274:         })}
275:     </div>
276:   );
277: }
278: function getPayloadConfigFromPayload(
279:   config: ChartConfig,
280:   payload: unknown,
281:   key: string
282: ) {
283:   if (typeof payload !== "object" || payload === null) {
284:     return undefined;
285:   }
286:   const payloadPayload =
287:     "payload" in payload &&
288:     typeof payload.payload === "object" &&
289:     payload.payload !== null
290:       ? payload.payload
291:       : undefined;
292:   let configLabelKey: string = key;
293:   if (
294:     key in payload &&
295:     typeof payload[key as keyof typeof payload] === "string"
296:   ) {
297:     configLabelKey = payload[key as keyof typeof payload] as string;
298:   } else if (
299:     payloadPayload &&
300:     key in payloadPayload &&
301:     typeof payloadPayload[key as keyof typeof payloadPayload] === "string"
302:   ) {
303:     configLabelKey = payloadPayload[
304:       key as keyof typeof payloadPayload
305:     ] as string;
306:   }
307:   return configLabelKey in config
308:     ? config[configLabelKey]
309:     : config[key as keyof typeof config];
310: }

313:   ChartTooltip,

  1: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
  2: import * as DialogPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog";
  3: import { XIcon } from "lucide-react";
  4: import * as React from "react";
  5: const DialogCompositionContext = React.createContext<{
  6:   isComposing: () => boolean;
  7:   setComposing: (composing: boolean) => void;
  8:   justEndedComposing: () => boolean;
  9:   markCompositionEnd: () => void;
 10: }>({
 11:   isComposing: () => false,
 12:   setComposing: () => {},
 13:   justEndedComposing: () => false,
 14:   markCompositionEnd: () => {},
 15: });
 16: export const useDialogComposition = () =>
 17:   React.useContext(DialogCompositionContext);
 18: function Dialog({
 19:   ...props
 20: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Root>) {
 21:   const composingRef = React.useRef(false);
 22:   const justEndedRef = React.useRef(false);
 23:   const endTimerRef = React.useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>(null);
 24:   const contextValue = React.useMemo(
 25:     () => ({
 26:       isComposing: () => composingRef.current,
 27:       setComposing: (composing: boolean) => {
 28:         composingRef.current = composing;
 29:       },
 30:       justEndedComposing: () => justEndedRef.current,
 31:       markCompositionEnd: () => {
 32:         justEndedRef.current = true;
 33:         if (endTimerRef.current) {
 34:           clearTimeout(endTimerRef.current);
 35:         }
 36:         endTimerRef.current = setTimeout(() => {
 37:           justEndedRef.current = false;
 38:         }, 150);
 39:       },
 40:     }),
 41:     []
 42:   );
 43:   return (
 44:     <DialogCompositionContext.Provider value={contextValue}>
 45:       <DialogPrimitive.Root data-slot="dialog" {...props} />
 46:     </DialogCompositionContext.Provider>
 47:   );
 48: }
 49: function DialogTrigger({
 50:   ...props
 51: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Trigger>) {
 52:   return <DialogPrimitive.Trigger data-slot="dialog-trigger" {...props} />;
 53: }
 54: function DialogPortal({
 55:   ...props
 56: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Portal>) {
 57:   return <DialogPrimitive.Portal data-slot="dialog-portal" {...props} />;
 58: }
 59: function DialogClose({
 60:   ...props
 61: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Close>) {
 62:   return <DialogPrimitive.Close data-slot="dialog-close" {...props} />;
 63: }
 64: function DialogOverlay({
 65:   className,
 66:   ...props
 67: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>) {
 68:   return (
 69:     <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
 70:       data-slot="dialog-overlay"
 71:       className={cn(
 72:         "data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/50",
 73:         className
 74:       )}
 75:       {...props}
 76:     />
 77:   );
 78: }
 79: DialogOverlay.displayName = "DialogOverlay";
 80: function DialogContent({
 81:   className,
 82:   children,
 83:   showCloseButton = true,
 84:   onEscapeKeyDown,
 85:   ...props
 86: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content> & {
 87:   showCloseButton?: boolean;
 88: }) {
 89:   const { isComposing } = useDialogComposition();
 90:   const handleEscapeKeyDown = React.useCallback(
 91:     (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
 92:       const isCurrentlyComposing = (e as any).isComposing || isComposing();
 93:       if (isCurrentlyComposing) {
 94:         e.preventDefault();
 95:         return;
 96:       }
 97:       onEscapeKeyDown?.(e);
 98:     },
 99:     [isComposing, onEscapeKeyDown]
100:   );
101:   return (
102:     <DialogPortal data-slot="dialog-portal">
103:       <DialogOverlay />
104:       <DialogPrimitive.Content
105:         data-slot="dialog-content"
106:         className={cn(
107:           "bg-background data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 fixed top-[50%] left-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-[calc(100%-2rem)] translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 rounded-lg border p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 sm:max-w-lg",
108:           className
109:         )}
110:         onEscapeKeyDown={handleEscapeKeyDown}
111:         {...props}
112:       >
113:         {children}
114:         {showCloseButton && (
115:           <DialogPrimitive.Close
116:             data-slot="dialog-close"
117:             className="ring-offset-background focus:ring-ring data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground absolute top-4 right-4 rounded-xs opacity-70 transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2 focus:outline-hidden disabled:pointer-events-none [&_svg]:pointer-events-none [&_svg]:shrink-0 [&_svg:not([class*='size-'])]:size-4"
118:           >
119:             <XIcon />
120:             <span className="sr-only">Close</span>
121:           </DialogPrimitive.Close>
122:         )}
123:       </DialogPrimitive.Content>
124:     </DialogPortal>
125:   );
126: }
127: function DialogHeader({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
128:   return (
129:     <div
130:       data-slot="dialog-header"
131:       className={cn("flex flex-col gap-2 text-center sm:text-left", className)}
132:       {...props}
133:     />
134:   );

172: function FieldError({
173:   className,
174:   children,
175:   errors,
176:   ...props
177: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
178:   errors?: Array<{ message?: string } | undefined>;
179: }) {
180:   const content = useMemo(() => {
181:     if (children) {
182:       return children;
183:     }
184:     if (!errors) {
185:       return null;
186:     }
187:     if (errors?.length === 1 && errors[0]?.message) {
188:       return errors[0].message;
189:     }
190:     return (
191:       <ul className="ml-4 flex list-disc flex-col gap-1">
192:         {errors.map(
193:           (error, index) =>
194:             error?.message && <li key={index}>{error.message}</li>
195:         )}
196:       </ul>
197:     );
198:   }, [children, errors]);
199:   if (!content) {
200:     return null;
201:   }
202:   return (
203:     <div
204:       role="alert"
205:       data-slot="field-error"
206:       className={cn("text-destructive text-sm font-normal", className)}
207:       {...props}
208:     >
209:       {content}
210:     </div>
211:   );
212: }

224: };

  1: "use client";
  2: import * as React from "react";
  3: import * as LabelPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-label";
  4: import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot";
  5: import {
  6:   Controller,
  7:   FormProvider,
  8:   useFormContext,
  9:   useFormState,
 10:   type ControllerProps,
 11:   type FieldPath,
 12:   type FieldValues,
 13: } from "react-hook-form";
 14: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 15: import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label";
 16: const Form = FormProvider;
 17: type FormFieldContextValue<
 18:   TFieldValues extends FieldValues = FieldValues,
 19:   TName extends FieldPath<TFieldValues> = FieldPath<TFieldValues>,
 20: > = {
 21:   name: TName;
 22: };
 23: const FormFieldContext = React.createContext<FormFieldContextValue>(
 24:   {} as FormFieldContextValue
 25: );
 26: const FormField = <
 27:   TFieldValues extends FieldValues = FieldValues,
 28:   TName extends FieldPath<TFieldValues> = FieldPath<TFieldValues>,
 29: >({
 30:   ...props
 31: }: ControllerProps<TFieldValues, TName>) => {
 32:   return (
 33:     <FormFieldContext.Provider value={{ name: props.name }}>
 34:       <Controller {...props} />
 35:     </FormFieldContext.Provider>
 36:   );
 37: };
 38: const useFormField = () => {
 39:   const fieldContext = React.useContext(FormFieldContext);
 40:   const itemContext = React.useContext(FormItemContext);
 41:   const { getFieldState } = useFormContext();
 42:   const formState = useFormState({ name: fieldContext.name });
 43:   const fieldState = getFieldState(fieldContext.name, formState);
 44:   if (!fieldContext) {
 45:     throw new Error("useFormField should be used within <FormField>");
 46:   }
 47:   const { id } = itemContext;
 48:   return {
 49:     id,
 50:     name: fieldContext.name,
 51:     formItemId: `${id}-form-item`,
 52:     formDescriptionId: `${id}-form-item-description`,
 53:     formMessageId: `${id}-form-item-message`,
 54:     ...fieldState,
 55:   };
 56: };
 57: type FormItemContextValue = {
 58:   id: string;
 59: };
 60: const FormItemContext = React.createContext<FormItemContextValue>(
 61:   {} as FormItemContextValue
 62: );
 63: function FormItem({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
 64:   const id = React.useId();
 65:   return (
 66:     <FormItemContext.Provider value={{ id }}>
 67:       <div
 68:         data-slot="form-item"
 69:         className={cn("grid gap-2", className)}
 70:         {...props}
 71:       />
 72:     </FormItemContext.Provider>
 73:   );
 74: }
 75: function FormLabel({
 76:   className,
 77:   ...props
 78: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof LabelPrimitive.Root>) {
 79:   const { error, formItemId } = useFormField();
 80:   return (
 81:     <Label
 82:       data-slot="form-label"
 83:       data-error={!!error}
 84:       className={cn("data-[error=true]:text-destructive", className)}
 85:       htmlFor={formItemId}
 86:       {...props}
 87:     />
 88:   );
 89: }
 90: function FormControl({ ...props }: React.ComponentProps<typeof Slot>) {
 91:   const { error, formItemId, formDescriptionId, formMessageId } =
 92:     useFormField();
 93:   return (
 94:     <Slot
 95:       data-slot="form-control"
 96:       id={formItemId}
 97:       aria-describedby={
 98:         !error
 99:           ? `${formDescriptionId}`
100:           : `${formDescriptionId} ${formMessageId}`
101:       }
102:       aria-invalid={!!error}
103:       {...props}
104:     />
105:   );
106: }
107: function FormDescription({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"p">) {
108:   const { formDescriptionId } = useFormField();
109:   return (
110:     <p
111:       data-slot="form-description"
112:       id={formDescriptionId}
113:       className={cn("text-muted-foreground text-sm", className)}
114:       {...props}
115:     />
116:   );
117: }
118: function FormMessage({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"p">) {
119:   const { error, formMessageId } = useFormField();
120:   const body = error ? String(error?.message ?? "") : props.children;
121:   if (!body) {
122:     return null;
123:   }
124:   return (
125:     <p
126:       data-slot="form-message"
127:       id={formMessageId}
128:       className={cn("text-destructive text-sm", className)}
129:       {...props}
130:     >
131:       {body}
132:     </p>
133:   );
134: }
135: export {
136:   useFormField,
137:   Form,
138:   FormItem,
139:   FormLabel,
140:   FormControl,
141:   FormDescription,
142:   FormMessage,
143:   FormField,
144: };

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/client/src/components/ui/input.tsx

 1: import { useDialogComposition } from "@/components/ui/dialog";
 2: import { useComposition } from "@/hooks/useComposition";
 3: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 4: import * as React from "react";
 5: function Input({
 6:   className,
 7:   type,
 8:   onKeyDown,
 9:   onCompositionStart,
10:   onCompositionEnd,
11:   ...props
12: }: React.ComponentProps<"input">) {
13:   const dialogComposition = useDialogComposition();
14:   const {
15:     onCompositionStart: handleCompositionStart,
16:     onCompositionEnd: handleCompositionEnd,
17:     onKeyDown: handleKeyDown,
18:   } = useComposition<HTMLInputElement>({
19:     onKeyDown: (e) => {
20:       const isComposing = (e.nativeEvent as any).isComposing || dialogComposition.justEndedComposing();
21:       if (e.key === "Enter" && isComposing) {
22:         return;
23:       }
24:       onKeyDown?.(e);
25:     },
26:     onCompositionStart: e => {
27:       dialogComposition.setComposing(true);
28:       onCompositionStart?.(e);
29:     },
30:     onCompositionEnd: e => {
31:       dialogComposition.markCompositionEnd();
32:       setTimeout(() => {
33:         dialogComposition.setComposing(false);
34:       }, 100);
35:       onCompositionEnd?.(e);
36:     },
37:   });
38:   return (
39:     <input
40:       type={type}
41:       data-slot="input"
42:       className={cn(
43:         "file:text-foreground placeholder:text-muted-foreground selection:bg-primary selection:text-primary-foreground dark:bg-input/30 border-input h-9 w-full min-w-0 rounded-md border bg-transparent px-3 py-1 text-base shadow-xs transition-[color,box-shadow] outline-none file:inline-flex file:h-7 file:border-0 file:bg-transparent file:text-sm file:font-medium disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50 md:text-sm",
44:         "focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px]",
45:         "aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive",
46:         className
47:       )}
48:       onCompositionStart={handleCompositionStart}
49:       onCompositionEnd={handleCompositionEnd}
50:       onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
51:       {...props}
52:     />
53:   );
54: }
55: export { Input };

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/client/src/components/ui/sidebar.tsx
================
  1: "use client";
  2: import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
  3: import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
  4: import { Separator } from "@/components/ui/separator";
  5: import {
  6:   Sheet,
  7:   SheetContent,
  8:   SheetDescription,
  9:   SheetHeader,
 10:   SheetTitle,
 11: } from "@/components/ui/sheet";
 12: import { Skeleton } from "@/components/ui/skeleton";
 13: import {
 14:   Tooltip,
 15:   TooltipContent,
 16:   TooltipProvider,
 17:   TooltipTrigger,
 18: } from "@/components/ui/tooltip";
 19: import { useIsMobile } from "@/hooks/useMobile";
 20: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 21: import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot";
 22: import { cva, VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority";
 23: import { PanelLeftIcon } from "lucide-react";
 24: import * as React from "react";
 25: const SIDEBAR_COOKIE_NAME = "sidebar_state";
 26: const SIDEBAR_COOKIE_MAX_AGE = 60 * 60 * 24 * 7;
 27: const SIDEBAR_WIDTH = "16rem";
 28: const SIDEBAR_WIDTH_MOBILE = "18rem";
 29: const SIDEBAR_WIDTH_ICON = "3rem";
 30: const SIDEBAR_KEYBOARD_SHORTCUT = "b";
 31: type SidebarContextProps = {
 32:   state: "expanded" | "collapsed";
 33:   open: boolean;
 34:   setOpen: (open: boolean) => void;
 35:   openMobile: boolean;
 36:   setOpenMobile: (open: boolean) => void;
 37:   isMobile: boolean;
 38:   toggleSidebar: () => void;
 39: };
 40: const SidebarContext = React.createContext<SidebarContextProps | null>(null);
 41: function useSidebar() {
 42:   const context = React.useContext(SidebarContext);
 43:   if (!context) {
 44:     throw new Error("useSidebar must be used within a SidebarProvider.");
 45:   }
 46:   return context;
 47: }
 48: function SidebarProvider({
 49:   defaultOpen = true,
 50:   open: openProp,
 51:   onOpenChange: setOpenProp,
 52:   className,
 53:   style,
 54:   children,
 55:   ...props
 56: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
 57:   defaultOpen?: boolean;
 58:   open?: boolean;
 59:   onOpenChange?: (open: boolean) => void;
 60: }) {
 61:   const isMobile = useIsMobile();
 62:   const [openMobile, setOpenMobile] = React.useState(false);
 63:   const [_open, _setOpen] = React.useState(defaultOpen);
 64:   const open = openProp ?? _open;
 65:   const setOpen = React.useCallback(
 66:     (value: boolean | ((value: boolean) => boolean)) => {
 67:       const openState = typeof value === "function" ? value(open) : value;
 68:       if (setOpenProp) {
 69:         setOpenProp(openState);
 70:       } else {
 71:         _setOpen(openState);
 72:       }
 73:       document.cookie = `${SIDEBAR_COOKIE_NAME}=${openState}; path=/; max-age=${SIDEBAR_COOKIE_MAX_AGE}`;
 74:     },
 75:     [setOpenProp, open]
 76:   );
 77:   const toggleSidebar = React.useCallback(() => {
 78:     return isMobile ? setOpenMobile(open => !open) : setOpen(open => !open);
 79:   }, [isMobile, setOpen, setOpenMobile]);
 80:   React.useEffect(() => {
 81:     const handleKeyDown = (event: KeyboardEvent) => {
 82:       if (
 83:         event.key === SIDEBAR_KEYBOARD_SHORTCUT &&
 84:         (event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey)
 85:       ) {
 86:         event.preventDefault();
 87:         toggleSidebar();
 88:       }
 89:     };
 90:     window.addEventListener("keydown", handleKeyDown);
 91:     return () => window.removeEventListener("keydown", handleKeyDown);
 92:   }, [toggleSidebar]);
 93:   const state = open ? "expanded" : "collapsed";
 94:   const contextValue = React.useMemo<SidebarContextProps>(
 95:     () => ({
 96:       state,
 97:       open,
 98:       setOpen,
 99:       isMobile,
100:       openMobile,
101:       setOpenMobile,
102:       toggleSidebar,
103:     }),
104:     [state, open, setOpen, isMobile, openMobile, setOpenMobile, toggleSidebar]
105:   );
106:   return (
107:     <SidebarContext.Provider value={contextValue}>
108:       <TooltipProvider delayDuration={0}>
109:         <div
110:           data-slot="sidebar-wrapper"
111:           style={
112:             {
113:               "--sidebar-width": SIDEBAR_WIDTH,
114:               "--sidebar-width-icon": SIDEBAR_WIDTH_ICON,
115:               ...style,
116:             } as React.CSSProperties
117:           }
118:           className={cn(
119:             "group/sidebar-wrapper has-data-[variant=inset]:bg-sidebar flex min-h-svh w-full",
120:             className
121:           )}
122:           {...props}
123:         >
124:           {children}
125:         </div>
126:       </TooltipProvider>
127:     </SidebarContext.Provider>
128:   );
129: }
130: function Sidebar({
131:   side = "left",
132:   variant = "sidebar",
133:   collapsible = "offcanvas",
134:   disableTransition = false,
135:   className,
136:   children,
137:   ...props
138: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
139:   side?: "left" | "right";
140:   variant?: "sidebar" | "floating" | "inset";
141:   collapsible?: "offcanvas" | "icon" | "none";
142:   disableTransition?: boolean;
143: }) {
144:   const { isMobile, state, openMobile, setOpenMobile } = useSidebar();
145:   if (collapsible === "none") {
146:     return (
147:       <div
148:         data-slot="sidebar"
149:         className={cn(
150:           "bg-sidebar text-sidebar-foreground flex h-full w-(--sidebar-width) flex-col",
151:           className
152:         )}
153:         {...props}
154:       >
155:         {children}
156:       </div>
157:     );
158:   }
159:   if (isMobile) {
160:     return (
161:       <Sheet open={openMobile} onOpenChange={setOpenMobile} {...props}>
162:         <SheetContent
163:           data-sidebar="sidebar"
164:           data-slot="sidebar"
165:           data-mobile="true"
166:           className="bg-sidebar text-sidebar-foreground w-(--sidebar-width) p-0 [&>button]:hidden"
167:           style={
168:             {
169:               "--sidebar-width": SIDEBAR_WIDTH_MOBILE,
170:             } as React.CSSProperties
171:           }
172:           side={side}
173:         >
174:           <SheetHeader className="sr-only">
175:             <SheetTitle>Sidebar</SheetTitle>
176:             <SheetDescription>Displays the mobile sidebar.</SheetDescription>
177:           </SheetHeader>
178:           <div className="flex h-full w-full flex-col">{children}</div>
179:         </SheetContent>
180:       </Sheet>
181:     );
182:   }
183:   return (
184:     <div
185:       className="group peer text-sidebar-foreground hidden md:block"
186:       data-state={state}
187:       data-collapsible={state === "collapsed" ? collapsible : ""}
188:       data-variant={variant}
189:       data-side={side}
190:       data-slot="sidebar"
191:     >
192:       {}
193:       <div
194:         data-slot="sidebar-gap"
195:         className={cn(
196:           "relative w-(--sidebar-width) bg-transparent",
197:           disableTransition
198:             ? "transition-none"
199:             : "transition-[width] duration-200 ease-linear",
200:           "group-data-[collapsible=offcanvas]:w-0",
201:           "group-data-[side=right]:rotate-180",
202:           variant === "floating" || variant === "inset"
203:             ? "group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-[calc(var(--sidebar-width-icon)+(--spacing(4)))]"
204:             : "group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-(--sidebar-width-icon)"
205:         )}
206:       />
207:       <div
208:         data-slot="sidebar-container"
209:         className={cn(
210:           "fixed inset-y-0 z-10 hidden h-svh w-(--sidebar-width) md:flex",
211:           disableTransition
212:             ? "transition-none"
213:             : "transition-[left,right,width] duration-200 ease-linear",
214:           side === "left"
215:             ? "left-0 group-data-[collapsible=offcanvas]:left-[calc(var(--sidebar-width)*-1)]"
216:             : "right-0 group-data-[collapsible=offcanvas]:right-[calc(var(--sidebar-width)*-1)]",
217:           variant === "floating" || variant === "inset"
218:             ? "p-2 group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-[calc(var(--sidebar-width-icon)+(--spacing(4))+2px)]"
219:             : "group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-(--sidebar-width-icon) group-data-[side=left]:border-r group-data-[side=right]:border-l",
220:           className
221:         )}
222:         {...props}
223:       >
224:         <div
225:           data-sidebar="sidebar"
226:           data-slot="sidebar-inner"
227:           className="bg-sidebar group-data-[variant=floating]:border-sidebar-border flex h-full w-full flex-col group-data-[variant=floating]:rounded-lg group-data-[variant=floating]:border group-data-[variant=floating]:shadow-sm"
228:         >
229:           {children}
230:         </div>
231:       </div>
232:     </div>
233:   );
234: }
235: function SidebarTrigger({

457: function SidebarMenuButton({
458:   asChild = false,
459:   isActive = false,
460:   variant = "default",
461:   size = "default",
462:   tooltip,
463:   className,
464:   ...props
465: }: React.ComponentProps<"button"> & {
466:   asChild?: boolean;
467:   isActive?: boolean;
468:   tooltip?: string | React.ComponentProps<typeof TooltipContent>;
469: } & VariantProps<typeof sidebarMenuButtonVariants>) {
470:   const Comp = asChild ? Slot : "button";
471:   const { isMobile, state } = useSidebar();
472:   const button = (
473:     <Comp
474:       data-slot="sidebar-menu-button"
475:       data-sidebar="menu-button"
476:       data-size={size}
477:       data-active={isActive}
478:       className={cn(sidebarMenuButtonVariants({ variant, size }), className)}
479:       {...props}
480:     />
481:   );
482:   if (!tooltip) {
483:     return button;
484:   }
485:   if (typeof tooltip === "string") {
486:     tooltip = {
487:       children: tooltip,
488:     };
489:   }
490:   return (
491:     <Tooltip>
492:       <TooltipTrigger asChild>{button}</TooltipTrigger>
493:       <TooltipContent
494:         side="right"
495:         align="center"
496:         hidden={state !== "collapsed" || isMobile}
497:         {...tooltip}
498:       />
499:     </Tooltip>
500:   );
501: }

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/client/src/components/ui/slider.tsx

 1: import * as React from "react";
 2: import * as SliderPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-slider";
 3: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 4: function Slider({
 5:   className,
 6:   defaultValue,
 7:   value,
 8:   min = 0,
 9:   max = 100,
10:   ...props
11: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof SliderPrimitive.Root>) {
12:   const _values = React.useMemo(
13:     () =>
14:       Array.isArray(value)
15:         ? value
16:         : Array.isArray(defaultValue)
17:           ? defaultValue
18:           : [min, max],
19:     [value, defaultValue, min, max]
20:   );
21:   return (
22:     <SliderPrimitive.Root
23:       data-slot="slider"
24:       defaultValue={defaultValue}
25:       value={value}
26:       min={min}
27:       max={max}
28:       className={cn(
29:         "relative flex w-full touch-none items-center select-none data-[disabled]:opacity-50 data-[orientation=vertical]:h-full data-[orientation=vertical]:min-h-44 data-[orientation=vertical]:w-auto data-[orientation=vertical]:flex-col",
30:         className
31:       )}
32:       {...props}
33:     >
34:       <SliderPrimitive.Track
35:         data-slot="slider-track"
36:         className={cn(
37:           "bg-muted relative grow overflow-hidden rounded-full data-[orientation=horizontal]:h-1.5 data-[orientation=horizontal]:w-full data-[orientation=vertical]:h-full data-[orientation=vertical]:w-1.5"
38:         )}
39:       >
40:         <SliderPrimitive.Range
41:           data-slot="slider-range"
42:           className={cn(
43:             "bg-primary absolute data-[orientation=horizontal]:h-full data-[orientation=vertical]:w-full"
44:           )}
45:         />
46:       </SliderPrimitive.Track>
47:       {Array.from({ length: _values.length }, (_, index) => (
48:         <SliderPrimitive.Thumb
49:           data-slot="slider-thumb"
50:           key={index}
51:           className="border-primary ring-ring/50 block size-4 shrink-0 rounded-full border bg-white shadow-sm transition-[color,box-shadow] hover:ring-4 focus-visible:ring-4 focus-visible:outline-hidden disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50"
52:         />
53:       ))}
54:     </SliderPrimitive.Root>
55:   );
56: }
57: export { Slider };

 1: import { useDialogComposition } from "@/components/ui/dialog";
 2: import { useComposition } from "@/hooks/useComposition";
 3: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 4: import * as React from "react";
 5: function Textarea({
 6:   className,
 7:   onKeyDown,
 8:   onCompositionStart,
 9:   onCompositionEnd,
10:   ...props
11: }: React.ComponentProps<"textarea">) {
12:   const dialogComposition = useDialogComposition();
13:   const {
14:     onCompositionStart: handleCompositionStart,
15:     onCompositionEnd: handleCompositionEnd,
16:     onKeyDown: handleKeyDown,
17:   } = useComposition<HTMLTextAreaElement>({
18:     onKeyDown: (e) => {
19:       const isComposing = (e.nativeEvent as any).isComposing || dialogComposition.justEndedComposing();
20:       if (e.key === "Enter" && !e.shiftKey && isComposing) {
21:         return;
22:       }
23:       onKeyDown?.(e);
24:     },
25:     onCompositionStart: e => {
26:       dialogComposition.setComposing(true);
27:       onCompositionStart?.(e);
28:     },
29:     onCompositionEnd: e => {
30:       dialogComposition.markCompositionEnd();
31:       setTimeout(() => {
32:         dialogComposition.setComposing(false);
33:       }, 100);
34:       onCompositionEnd?.(e);
35:     },
36:   });
37:   return (
38:     <textarea
39:       data-slot="textarea"
40:       className={cn(
41:         "border-input placeholder:text-muted-foreground focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive dark:bg-input/30 flex field-sizing-content min-h-16 w-full rounded-md border bg-transparent px-3 py-2 text-base shadow-xs transition-[color,box-shadow] outline-none focus-visible:ring-[3px] disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50 md:text-sm",
42:         className
43:       )}
44:       onCompositionStart={handleCompositionStart}
45:       onCompositionEnd={handleCompositionEnd}
46:       onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
47:       {...props}
48:     />
49:   );
50: }
51: export { Textarea };

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/client/src/components/AIChatBox.tsx
================
  1: import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
  2: import { Textarea } from "@/components/ui/textarea";
  3: import { ScrollArea } from "@/components/ui/scroll-area";
  4: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
  5: import { Loader2, Send, User, Sparkles } from "lucide-react";
  6: import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from "react";
  7: import { Streamdown } from "streamdown";
  8: export type Message = {
  9:   role: "system" | "user" | "assistant";
 10:   content: string;
 11: };
 12: export type AIChatBoxProps = {
 13:   messages: Message[];
 14:   onSendMessage: (content: string) => void;
 15:   isLoading?: boolean;
 16:   placeholder?: string;
 17:   className?: string;
 18:   height?: string | number;
 19:   emptyStateMessage?: string;
 20:   suggestedPrompts?: string[];
 21: };
 22: export function AIChatBox({
 23:   messages,
 24:   onSendMessage,
 25:   isLoading = false,
 26:   placeholder = "Type your message...",
 27:   className,
 28:   height = "600px",
 29:   emptyStateMessage = "Start a conversation with AI",
 30:   suggestedPrompts,
 31: }: AIChatBoxProps) {
 32:   const [input, setInput] = useState("");
 33:   const scrollAreaRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
 34:   const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
 35:   const inputAreaRef = useRef<HTMLFormElement>(null);
 36:   const textareaRef = useRef<HTMLTextAreaElement>(null);
 37:   // Filter out system messages
 38:   const displayMessages = messages.filter((msg) => msg.role !== "system");
 39:   const [minHeightForLastMessage, setMinHeightForLastMessage] = useState(0);
 40:   useEffect(() => {
 41:     if (containerRef.current && inputAreaRef.current) {
 42:       const containerHeight = containerRef.current.offsetHeight;
 43:       const inputHeight = inputAreaRef.current.offsetHeight;
 44:       const scrollAreaHeight = containerHeight - inputHeight;
 45:       const userMessageReservedHeight = 56;
 46:       const calculatedHeight = scrollAreaHeight - 32 - userMessageReservedHeight;
 47:       setMinHeightForLastMessage(Math.max(0, calculatedHeight));
 48:     }
 49:   }, []);
 50:   const scrollToBottom = () => {
 51:     const viewport = scrollAreaRef.current?.querySelector(
 52:       '[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]'
 53:     ) as HTMLDivElement;
 54:     if (viewport) {
 55:       requestAnimationFrame(() => {
 56:         viewport.scrollTo({
 57:           top: viewport.scrollHeight,
 58:           behavior: 'smooth'
 59:         });
 60:       });
 61:     }
 62:   };
 63:   const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
 64:     e.preventDefault();
 65:     const trimmedInput = input.trim();
 66:     if (!trimmedInput || isLoading) return;
 67:     onSendMessage(trimmedInput);
 68:     setInput("");
 69:     // Scroll immediately after sending
 70:     scrollToBottom();
 71:     // Keep focus on input
 72:     textareaRef.current?.focus();
 73:   };
 74:   const handleKeyDown = (e: React.KeyboardEvent<HTMLTextAreaElement>) => {
 75:     if (e.key === "Enter" && !e.shiftKey) {
 76:       e.preventDefault();
 77:       handleSubmit(e);
 78:     }
 79:   };
 80:   return (
 81:     <div
 82:       ref={containerRef}
 83:       className={cn(
 84:         "flex flex-col bg-card text-card-foreground rounded-lg border shadow-sm",
 85:         className
 86:       )}
 87:       style={{ height }}
 88:     >
 89:       {}
 90:       <div ref={scrollAreaRef} className="flex-1 overflow-hidden">
 91:         {displayMessages.length === 0 ? (
 92:           <div className="flex h-full flex-col p-4">
 93:             <div className="flex flex-1 flex-col items-center justify-center gap-6 text-muted-foreground">
 94:               <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-3">
 95:                 <Sparkles className="size-12 opacity-20" />
 96:                 <p className="text-sm">{emptyStateMessage}</p>
 97:               </div>
 98:               {suggestedPrompts && suggestedPrompts.length > 0 && (
 99:                 <div className="flex max-w-2xl flex-wrap justify-center gap-2">
100:                   {suggestedPrompts.map((prompt, index) => (
101:                     <button
102:                       key={index}
103:                       onClick={() => onSendMessage(prompt)}
104:                       disabled={isLoading}
105:                       className="rounded-lg border border-border bg-card px-4 py-2 text-sm transition-colors hover:bg-accent disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50"
106:                     >
107:                       {prompt}
108:                     </button>
109:                   ))}
110:                 </div>
111:               )}
112:             </div>
113:           </div>
114:         ) : (
115:           <ScrollArea className="h-full">
116:             <div className="flex flex-col space-y-4 p-4">
117:               {displayMessages.map((message, index) => {
118:                 const isLastMessage = index === displayMessages.length - 1;
119:                 const shouldApplyMinHeight =
120:                   isLastMessage && !isLoading && minHeightForLastMessage > 0;
121:                 return (
122:                   <div
123:                     key={index}
124:                     className={cn(
125:                       "flex gap-3",
126:                       message.role === "user"
127:                         ? "justify-end items-start"
128:                         : "justify-start items-start"
129:                     )}
130:                     style={
131:                       shouldApplyMinHeight
132:                         ? { minHeight: `${minHeightForLastMessage}px` }
133:                         : undefined
134:                     }
135:                   >
136:                     {message.role === "assistant" && (
137:                       <div className="size-8 shrink-0 mt-1 rounded-full bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center">
138:                         <Sparkles className="size-4 text-primary" />
139:                       </div>
140:                     )}
141:                     <div
142:                       className={cn(
143:                         "max-w-[80%] rounded-lg px-4 py-2.5",
144:                         message.role === "user"
145:                           ? "bg-primary text-primary-foreground"
146:                           : "bg-muted text-foreground"
147:                       )}
148:                     >
149:                       {message.role === "assistant" ? (
150:                         <div className="prose prose-sm dark:prose-invert max-w-none">
151:                           <Streamdown>{message.content}</Streamdown>
152:                         </div>
153:                       ) : (
154:                         <p className="whitespace-pre-wrap text-sm">
155:                           {message.content}
156:                         </p>
157:                       )}
158:                     </div>
159:                     {message.role === "user" && (
160:                       <div className="size-8 shrink-0 mt-1 rounded-full bg-secondary flex items-center justify-center">
161:                         <User className="size-4 text-secondary-foreground" />
162:                       </div>
163:                     )}
164:                   </div>
165:                 );
166:               })}
167:               {isLoading && (
168:                 <div
169:                   className="flex items-start gap-3"
170:                   style={
171:                     minHeightForLastMessage > 0
172:                       ? { minHeight: `${minHeightForLastMessage}px` }
173:                       : undefined
174:                   }
175:                 >
176:                   <div className="size-8 shrink-0 mt-1 rounded-full bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center">
177:                     <Sparkles className="size-4 text-primary" />
178:                   </div>
179:                   <div className="rounded-lg bg-muted px-4 py-2.5">
180:                     <Loader2 className="size-4 animate-spin text-muted-foreground" />
181:                   </div>
182:                 </div>
183:               )}
184:             </div>
185:           </ScrollArea>
186:         )}
187:       </div>
188:       {}
189:       <form
190:         ref={inputAreaRef}
191:         onSubmit={handleSubmit}
192:         className="flex gap-2 p-4 border-t bg-background/50 items-end"
193:       >
194:         <Textarea
195:           ref={textareaRef}
196:           value={input}
197:           onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value)}
198:           onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
199:           placeholder={placeholder}
200:           className="flex-1 max-h-32 resize-none min-h-9"
201:           rows={1}
202:         />
203:         <Button
204:           type="submit"
205:           size="icon"
206:           disabled={!input.trim() || isLoading}
207:           className="shrink-0 h-[38px] w-[38px]"
208:         >
209:           {isLoading ? (
210:             <Loader2 className="size-4 animate-spin" />
211:           ) : (
212:             <Send className="size-4" />
213:           )}
214:         </Button>
215:       </form>
216:     </div>
217:   );
218: }

  2: import {
  3:   Sidebar,

  7:   SidebarInset,

 24:   { icon: Settings2, label: "Page Status", path: "/admin/status" },
