 86: type DashboardLayoutContentProps = {
 87:   children: React.ReactNode;
 88:   setSidebarWidth: (width: number) => void;
 89: };
 90: function DashboardLayoutContent({
 91:   children,
 92:   setSidebarWidth,
 93: }: DashboardLayoutContentProps) {
 94:   const { user, logout } = useAuth();
 95:   const [location, setLocation] = useLocation();
 96:   const { state, toggleSidebar } = useSidebar();
 97:   const isCollapsed = state === "collapsed";
 98:   const [isResizing, setIsResizing] = useState(false);
 99:   const sidebarRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
100:   const activeMenuItem = menuItems.find(item => item.path === location);
101:   const isMobile = useIsMobile();
102:   useEffect(() => {
103:     if (isCollapsed) {
104:       setIsResizing(false);
105:     }
106:   }, [isCollapsed]);
107:   useEffect(() => {
108:     const handleMouseMove = (e: MouseEvent) => {
109:       if (!isResizing) return;
110:       const sidebarLeft = sidebarRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect().left ?? 0;
111:       const newWidth = e.clientX - sidebarLeft;
112:       if (newWidth >= MIN_WIDTH && newWidth <= MAX_WIDTH) {
113:         setSidebarWidth(newWidth);
114:       }
115:     };
116:     const handleMouseUp = () => {
117:       setIsResizing(false);
118:     };
119:     if (isResizing) {
120:       document.addEventListener("mousemove", handleMouseMove);
121:       document.addEventListener("mouseup", handleMouseUp);
122:       document.body.style.cursor = "col-resize";
123:       document.body.style.userSelect = "none";
124:     }
125:     return () => {
126:       document.removeEventListener("mousemove", handleMouseMove);
127:       document.removeEventListener("mouseup", handleMouseUp);
128:       document.body.style.cursor = "";
129:       document.body.style.userSelect = "";
130:     };
131:   }, [isResizing, setSidebarWidth]);
132:   return (
133:     <>
134:       <div className="relative" ref={sidebarRef}>
135:         <Sidebar collapsible="icon" className="border-r border-sidebar-border" disableTransition={isResizing}>
136:           <SidebarHeader className="border-b border-sidebar-border px-4 py-4">
137:             <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
138:               <button
139:                 onClick={toggleSidebar}
140:                 className="flex h-9 w-9 items-center justify-center border border-sidebar-border bg-sidebar text-sidebar-foreground transition-colors hover:bg-sidebar-accent hover:text-sidebar-accent-foreground focus:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-ring"
141:                 aria-label="Toggle navigation"
142:               >
143:                 <PanelLeft className="h-4 w-4" />
144:               </button>
145:               {!isCollapsed ? (
146:                 <div className="min-w-0">
147:                   <p className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-muted-foreground">
148:                     Owner dashboard
149:                   </p>
150:                   <h2 className="mt-2 text-sm font-semibold tracking-[0.02em] text-sidebar-foreground">
151:                     The Well Lived Citizen
152:                   </h2>
153:                 </div>
154:               ) : null}
155:             </div>
156:           </SidebarHeader>
157:           <SidebarContent className="gap-0 px-3 py-4">
158:             <SidebarMenu className="gap-2">
159:               {menuItems.map(item => {
160:                 const isActive = location === item.path;
161:                 return (
162:                   <SidebarMenuItem key={item.path}>
163:                     <SidebarMenuButton
164:                       isActive={isActive}
165:                       onClick={() => setLocation(item.path)}
166:                       tooltip={item.label}
167:                       className="!rounded-none border border-transparent px-3 py-3 text-sm font-medium shadow-none transition-colors hover:border-sidebar-border hover:bg-sidebar-accent hover:text-sidebar-accent-foreground data-[active=true]:border-sidebar-border data-[active=true]:bg-sidebar-accent data-[active=true]:text-sidebar-accent-foreground"
168:                     >
169:                       <item.icon className="h-4 w-4" />
170:                       <span>{item.label}</span>
171:                     </SidebarMenuButton>
172:                   </SidebarMenuItem>
173:                 );
174:               })}
175:             </SidebarMenu>
176:           </SidebarContent>
177:           <SidebarFooter className="border-t border-sidebar-border p-4">
178:             <div className="space-y-3">
179:               <div className="border border-sidebar-border bg-sidebar px-3 py-3 text-left">
180:                 <p className="text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-muted-foreground">
181:                   Signed in
182:                 </p>
183:                 <p className="mt-2 text-sm font-medium text-sidebar-foreground">{user?.name || "Owner"}</p>
184:                 <p className="mt-1 text-xs text-muted-foreground">{user?.email || "No email available"}</p>
185:               </div>
186:               <Button
187:                 onClick={logout}
188:                 variant="outline"
189:                 className="w-full !rounded-none border-sidebar-border bg-transparent text-foreground shadow-none hover:bg-sidebar-accent hover:text-sidebar-accent-foreground"
190:               >

198:           className={`absolute top-0 right-0 h-full w-px bg-sidebar-border ${isCollapsed ? "hidden" : "block"}`}
199:           onMouseDown={() => {
200:             if (isCollapsed) return;

202:           }}
203:           style={{ zIndex: 50 }}
204:         />

206:       <SidebarInset className="!rounded-none !shadow-none bg-background">

 1: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 2: import { AlertTriangle, RotateCcw } from "lucide-react";
 3: import { Component, ReactNode } from "react";
 4: interface Props {
 5:   children: ReactNode;
 6: }
 7: interface State {
 8:   hasError: boolean;
 9:   error: Error | null;
10: }
11: class ErrorBoundary extends Component<Props, State> {
12:   constructor(props: Props) {
13:     super(props);
14:     this.state = { hasError: false, error: null };
15:   }
16:   static getDerivedStateFromError(error: Error): State {
17:     return { hasError: true, error };
18:   }
19:   render() {
20:     if (this.state.hasError) {
21:       return (
22:         <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen p-8 bg-background">
23:           <div className="flex flex-col items-center w-full max-w-2xl p-8">
24:             <AlertTriangle
25:               size={48}
26:               className="text-destructive mb-6 flex-shrink-0"
27:             />
28:             <h2 className="text-xl mb-4">An unexpected error occurred.</h2>
29:             <div className="p-4 w-full rounded bg-muted overflow-auto mb-6">
30:               <pre className="text-sm text-muted-foreground whitespace-break-spaces">
31:                 {this.state.error?.stack}
32:               </pre>
33:             </div>
34:             <button
35:               onClick={() => window.location.reload()}
36:               className={cn(
37:                 "flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2 rounded-lg",
38:                 "bg-primary text-primary-foreground",
39:                 "hover:opacity-90 cursor-pointer"
40:               )}
41:             >
42:               <RotateCcw size={16} />
43:               Reload Page
44:             </button>
45:           </div>
46:         </div>
47:       );
48:     }
49:     return this.props.children;
50:   }
51: }
52: export default ErrorBoundary;

 1: import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
 2: import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
 3: import {
 4:   Dialog,
 5:   DialogContent,
 6:   DialogDescription,
 7:   DialogFooter,
 8:   DialogTitle,
 9: } from "@/components/ui/dialog";
10: interface ManusDialogProps {
11:   title?: string;
12:   logo?: string;
13:   open?: boolean;
14:   onLogin: () => void;
15:   onOpenChange?: (open: boolean) => void;
16:   onClose?: () => void;
17: }
18: export function ManusDialog({
19:   title,
20:   logo,
21:   open = false,
22:   onLogin,
23:   onOpenChange,
24:   onClose,
25: }: ManusDialogProps) {
26:   const [internalOpen, setInternalOpen] = useState(open);
27:   useEffect(() => {
28:     if (!onOpenChange) {
29:       setInternalOpen(open);
30:     }
31:   }, [open, onOpenChange]);
32:   const handleOpenChange = (nextOpen: boolean) => {
33:     if (onOpenChange) {
34:       onOpenChange(nextOpen);
35:     } else {
36:       setInternalOpen(nextOpen);
37:     }
38:     if (!nextOpen) {
39:       onClose?.();
40:     }
41:   };
42:   return (
43:     <Dialog
44:       open={onOpenChange ? open : internalOpen}
45:       onOpenChange={handleOpenChange}
46:     >
47:       <DialogContent className="py-5 bg-[#f8f8f7] rounded-[20px] w-[400px] shadow-[0px_4px_11px_0px_rgba(0,0,0,0.08)] border border-[rgba(0,0,0,0.08)] backdrop-blur-2xl p-0 gap-0 text-center">

50:             <div className="w-16 h-16 bg-white rounded-xl border border-[rgba(0,0,0,0.08)] flex items-center justify-center">
51:               <img
52:                 src={logo}
53:                 alt="Dialog graphic"
54:                 className="w-10 h-10 rounded-md"
55:               />
56:             </div>
57:           ) : null}
58:           {}

60:             <DialogTitle className="text-xl font-semibold text-[#34322d] leading-[26px] tracking-[-0.44px]">

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/client/src/components/Map.tsx
================
 1: import { useEffect, useRef } from "react";
 2: import { usePersistFn } from "@/hooks/usePersistFn";
 3: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 4: declare global {
 5:   interface Window {
 6:     google?: typeof google;
 7:   }
 8: }
 9: const API_KEY = import.meta.env.VITE_FRONTEND_FORGE_API_KEY;
10: const FORGE_BASE_URL =
11:   import.meta.env.VITE_FRONTEND_FORGE_API_URL ||
12:   "https://forge.butterfly-effect.dev";
13: const MAPS_PROXY_URL = `${FORGE_BASE_URL}/v1/maps/proxy`;
14: function loadMapScript() {
15:   return new Promise(resolve => {
16:     const script = document.createElement("script");
17:     script.src = `${MAPS_PROXY_URL}/maps/api/js?key=${API_KEY}&v=weekly&libraries=marker,places,geocoding,geometry`;
18:     script.async = true;
19:     script.crossOrigin = "anonymous";
20:     script.onload = () => {
21:       resolve(null);
22:       script.remove();
23:     };
24:     script.onerror = () => {
25:       console.error("Failed to load Google Maps script");
26:     };
27:     document.head.appendChild(script);
28:   });
29: }
30: interface MapViewProps {
31:   className?: string;
32:   initialCenter?: google.maps.LatLngLiteral;
33:   initialZoom?: number;
34:   onMapReady?: (map: google.maps.Map) => void;
35: }
36: export function MapView({
37:   className,
38:   initialCenter = { lat: 37.7749, lng: -122.4194 },
39:   initialZoom = 12,
40:   onMapReady,
41: }: MapViewProps) {
42:   const mapContainer = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
43:   const map = useRef<google.maps.Map | null>(null);
44:   const init = usePersistFn(async () => {
45:     await loadMapScript();
46:     if (!mapContainer.current) {
47:       console.error("Map container not found");
48:       return;
49:     }
50:     map.current = new window.google.maps.Map(mapContainer.current, {
51:       zoom: initialZoom,
52:       center: initialCenter,
53:       mapTypeControl: true,
54:       fullscreenControl: true,
55:       zoomControl: true,
56:       streetViewControl: true,
57:       mapId: "DEMO_MAP_ID",
58:     });
59:     if (onMapReady) {
60:       onMapReady(map.current);
61:     }
62:   });
63:   useEffect(() => {
64:     init();
65:   }, [init]);
66:   return (
67:     <div ref={mapContainer} className={cn("w-full h-[500px]", className)} />
68:   );
69: }

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/client/src/contexts/ThemeContext.tsx
================
 1: import React, { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState } from "react";
 2: type Theme = "light" | "dark";
 3: interface ThemeContextType {
 4:   theme: Theme;
 5:   toggleTheme?: () => void;
 6:   switchable: boolean;
 7: }
 8: const ThemeContext = createContext<ThemeContextType | undefined>(undefined);
 9: interface ThemeProviderProps {
10:   children: React.ReactNode;
11:   defaultTheme?: Theme;
12:   switchable?: boolean;
13: }
14: export function ThemeProvider({
15:   children,
16:   defaultTheme = "light",
17:   switchable = false,
18: }: ThemeProviderProps) {
19:   const [theme, setTheme] = useState<Theme>(() => {
20:     if (switchable) {
21:       const stored = localStorage.getItem("theme");
22:       return (stored as Theme) || defaultTheme;
23:     }
24:     return defaultTheme;
25:   });
26:   useEffect(() => {
27:     const root = document.documentElement;
28:     if (theme === "dark") {
29:       root.classList.add("dark");
30:     } else {
31:       root.classList.remove("dark");
32:     }
33:     if (switchable) {
34:       localStorage.setItem("theme", theme);
35:     }
36:   }, [theme, switchable]);
37:   const toggleTheme = switchable
38:     ? () => {
39:         setTheme(prev => (prev === "light" ? "dark" : "light"));
40:       }
41:     : undefined;
42:   return (
43:     <ThemeContext.Provider value={{ theme, toggleTheme, switchable }}>
44:       {children}
45:     </ThemeContext.Provider>
46:   );
47: }
48: export function useTheme() {
49:   const context = useContext(ThemeContext);
50:   if (!context) {
51:     throw new Error("useTheme must be used within ThemeProvider");
52:   }
53:   return context;
54: }

================
File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/client/src/hooks/useComposition.ts
================
 1: import { useRef } from "react";
 2: import { usePersistFn } from "./usePersistFn";
 3: export interface UseCompositionReturn<
 4:   T extends HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement,
 5: > {
 6:   onCompositionStart: React.CompositionEventHandler<T>;
 7:   onCompositionEnd: React.CompositionEventHandler<T>;
 8:   onKeyDown: React.KeyboardEventHandler<T>;
 9:   isComposing: () => boolean;
10: }
11: export interface UseCompositionOptions<
12:   T extends HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement,
13: > {
14:   onKeyDown?: React.KeyboardEventHandler<T>;
15:   onCompositionStart?: React.CompositionEventHandler<T>;
16:   onCompositionEnd?: React.CompositionEventHandler<T>;
17: }
18: type TimerResponse = ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>;
19: export function useComposition<
20:   T extends HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement = HTMLInputElement,
21: >(options: UseCompositionOptions<T> = {}): UseCompositionReturn<T> {
22:   const {
23:     onKeyDown: originalOnKeyDown,
24:     onCompositionStart: originalOnCompositionStart,
25:     onCompositionEnd: originalOnCompositionEnd,
26:   } = options;
27:   const c = useRef(false);
28:   const timer = useRef<TimerResponse | null>(null);
29:   const timer2 = useRef<TimerResponse | null>(null);
30:   const onCompositionStart = usePersistFn((e: React.CompositionEvent<T>) => {
31:     if (timer.current) {
32:       clearTimeout(timer.current);
33:       timer.current = null;
34:     }
35:     if (timer2.current) {
36:       clearTimeout(timer2.current);
37:       timer2.current = null;
38:     }
39:     c.current = true;
40:     originalOnCompositionStart?.(e);
41:   });
42:   const onCompositionEnd = usePersistFn((e: React.CompositionEvent<T>) => {
43:     timer.current = setTimeout(() => {
44:       timer2.current = setTimeout(() => {
45:         c.current = false;
46:       });
47:     });
48:     originalOnCompositionEnd?.(e);
49:   });
50:   const onKeyDown = usePersistFn((e: React.KeyboardEvent<T>) => {
51:     if (
52:       c.current &&
53:       (e.key === "Escape" || (e.key === "Enter" && !e.shiftKey))
54:     ) {
55:       e.stopPropagation();
56:       return;
57:     }
58:     originalOnKeyDown?.(e);
59:   });
60:   const isComposing = usePersistFn(() => {
61:     return c.current;
62:   });
63:   return {
64:     onCompositionStart,
65:     onCompositionEnd,
66:     onKeyDown,
67:     isComposing,
68:   };
69: }

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/client/src/hooks/useMobile.tsx
================
 1: import * as React from "react";
 2: const MOBILE_BREAKPOINT = 768;
 3: export function useIsMobile() {
 4:   const [isMobile, setIsMobile] = React.useState<boolean | undefined>(
 5:     undefined
 6:   );
 7:   React.useEffect(() => {
 8:     const mql = window.matchMedia(`(max-width: ${MOBILE_BREAKPOINT - 1}px)`);
 9:     const onChange = () => {
10:       setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT);
11:     };
12:     mql.addEventListener("change", onChange);
13:     setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT);
14:     return () => mql.removeEventListener("change", onChange);
15:   }, []);
16:   return !!isMobile;
17: }

================
File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/client/src/hooks/usePersistFn.ts
================
 1: import { useRef } from "react";
 2: type noop = (...args: any[]) => any;
 3: export function usePersistFn<T extends noop>(fn: T) {
 4:   const fnRef = useRef<T>(fn);
 5:   fnRef.current = fn;
 6:   const persistFn = useRef<T>(null);
 7:   if (!persistFn.current) {
 8:     persistFn.current = function (this: unknown, ...args) {
 9:       return fnRef.current!.apply(this, args);
10:     } as T;
11:   }
12:   return persistFn.current!;
13: }

3: export function cn(...inputs: ClassValue[]) {

In a real app, you would call a tRPC mutation here:\n\n\`\`\`typescript\nconst chatMutation = trpc.ai.chat.useMutation({\n  onSuccess: (response) => {\n    setChatMessages(prev => [...prev, {\n      role: "assistant",\n      content: response.choices[0].message.content\n    }]);\n  }\n});\n\nchatMutation.mutate({ messages: newMessages });\n\`\`\`\n\nYour message was: "${content}"`,
 215:       };

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/client/src/App.tsx

 1: import { Toaster } from "@/components/ui/sonner";
 2: import { TooltipProvider } from "@/components/ui/tooltip";
 3: import NotFound from "@/pages/NotFound";
 4: import { Route, Switch } from "wouter";
 5: import ErrorBoundary from "./components/ErrorBoundary";
 6: import { ThemeProvider } from "./contexts/ThemeContext";
 7: import AdminDashboard from "./pages/AdminDashboard";
 8: import AdminStatus from "./pages/AdminStatus";
 9: function Router() {
10:   return (
11:     <Switch>
12:       <Route path="/admin" component={AdminDashboard} />
13:       <Route path="/admin/status" component={AdminStatus} />
14:       <Route path="/404" component={NotFound} />
15:       <Route component={NotFound} />
16:     </Switch>
17:   );
18: }
19: function App() {
20:   return (
21:     <ErrorBoundary>
22:       <ThemeProvider defaultTheme="light">
23:         <TooltipProvider>
24:           <Toaster />
25:           <Router />
26:         </TooltipProvider>
27:       </ThemeProvider>
28:     </ErrorBoundary>
29:   );
30: }
31: export default App;

================
File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/client/src/const.ts
================
 1: export { COOKIE_NAME, ONE_YEAR_MS } from "@shared/const";
 2: export const getLoginUrl = () => {
 3:   const oauthPortalUrl = import.meta.env.VITE_OAUTH_PORTAL_URL;
 4:   const appId = import.meta.env.VITE_APP_ID;
 5:   const redirectUri = `${window.location.origin}/api/oauth/callback`;
 6:   const state = btoa(redirectUri);
 7:   const url = new URL(`${oauthPortalUrl}/app-auth`);
 8:   url.searchParams.set("appId", appId);
 9:   url.searchParams.set("redirectUri", redirectUri);
10:   url.searchParams.set("state", state);
11:   url.searchParams.set("type", "signIn");
12:   return url.toString();
13: };

================
File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/client/src/main.tsx
================
 1: import { trpc } from "@/lib/trpc";
 2: import { UNAUTHED_ERR_MSG } from '@shared/const';
 3: import { QueryClient, QueryClientProvider } from "@tanstack/react-query";
 4: import { httpBatchLink, TRPCClientError } from "@trpc/client";
 5: import { createRoot } from "react-dom/client";
 6: import superjson from "superjson";
 7: import App from "./App";
 8: import { getLoginUrl } from "./const";
 9: import "./index.css";
10: const queryClient = new QueryClient();
11: const redirectToLoginIfUnauthorized = (error: unknown) => {
12:   if (!(error instanceof TRPCClientError)) return;
13:   if (typeof window === "undefined") return;
14:   const isUnauthorized = error.message === UNAUTHED_ERR_MSG;
15:   if (!isUnauthorized) return;
16:   window.location.href = getLoginUrl();
17: };
18: queryClient.getQueryCache().subscribe(event => {
19:   if (event.type === "updated" && event.action.type === "error") {
20:     const error = event.query.state.error;
21:     redirectToLoginIfUnauthorized(error);
22:     console.error("[API Query Error]", error);
23:   }
24: });
25: queryClient.getMutationCache().subscribe(event => {
26:   if (event.type === "updated" && event.action.type === "error") {
27:     const error = event.mutation.state.error;
28:     redirectToLoginIfUnauthorized(error);
29:     console.error("[API Mutation Error]", error);
30:   }
31: });
32: const trpcClient = trpc.createClient({
33:   links: [
34:     httpBatchLink({
35:       url: "/api/trpc",
36:       transformer: superjson,
37:       fetch(input, init) {
38:         return globalThis.fetch(input, {
39:           ...(init ?? {}),
40:           credentials: "include",
41:         });
42:       },
43:     }),
44:   ],
45: });
46: createRoot(document.getElementById("root")!).render(
47:   <trpc.Provider client={trpcClient} queryClient={queryClient}>
48:     <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
49:       <App />
50:     </QueryClientProvider>
51:   </trpc.Provider>
52: );

 1: import { int, mysqlEnum, mysqlTable, text, timestamp, varchar } from "drizzle-orm/mysql-core";
 2: export const users = mysqlTable("users", {
 3:   id: int("id").autoincrement().primaryKey(),
 4:   openId: varchar("openId", { length: 64 }).notNull().unique(),
 5:   name: text("name"),
 6:   email: varchar("email", { length: 320 }),
 7:   loginMethod: varchar("loginMethod", { length: 64 }),
 8:   role: mysqlEnum("role", ["user", "admin"]).default("user").notNull(),
 9:   createdAt: timestamp("createdAt").defaultNow().notNull(),
10:   updatedAt: timestamp("updatedAt").defaultNow().onUpdateNow().notNull(),
11:   lastSignedIn: timestamp("lastSignedIn").defaultNow().notNull(),
12: });
13: export const businessInfo = mysqlTable("businessInfo", {
14:   id: int("id").autoincrement().primaryKey(),
15:   businessName: varchar("businessName", { length: 255 }).notNull().default("The Well Lived Citizen"),
16:   legalEntity: varchar("legalEntity", { length: 255 }).notNull().default("Well Dressed Citizen LLC"),
17:   city: varchar("city", { length: 255 }).notNull().default("Los Angeles"),
18:   serviceArea: text("serviceArea").notNull(),
19:   primaryPhone: varchar("primaryPhone", { length: 32 }).notNull(),
20:   primaryPhoneRaw: varchar("primaryPhoneRaw", { length: 32 }).notNull(),
21:   workingPhone: varchar("workingPhone", { length: 32 }).notNull(),
22:   workingPhoneRaw: varchar("workingPhoneRaw", { length: 32 }).notNull(),
23:   zellePhone: varchar("zellePhone", { length: 32 }).notNull(),
24:   zellePhoneRaw: varchar("zellePhoneRaw", { length: 32 }).notNull(),
25:   primaryEmail: varchar("primaryEmail", { length: 320 }).notNull(),
26:   zelleEmail: varchar("zelleEmail", { length: 320 }).notNull(),
27:   venmoHandle: varchar("venmoHandle", { length: 255 }).notNull(),
28:   stripePaymentLink: text("stripePaymentLink").notNull(),
29:   calendarLink: text("calendarLink").notNull(),
30:   instagramMain: text("instagramMain").notNull(),
31:   instagramCloset: text("instagramCloset").notNull(),
32:   instagramArchive: text("instagramArchive").notNull(),
33:   facebook: text("facebook").notNull(),
34:   poshmarkUrl: text("poshmarkUrl").notNull(),
35:   ebayUrl: text("ebayUrl").notNull(),
36:   responseTime: text("responseTime").notNull(),
37:   hoursNote: text("hoursNote").notNull(),
38:   paymentNote: text("paymentNote").notNull(),
39:   homeOrganizationSummary: text("homeOrganizationSummary").notNull(),
40:   legacySummary: text("legacySummary").notNull(),
41:   houseCallsSummary: text("houseCallsSummary").notNull(),
42:   resaleSummary: text("resaleSummary").notNull(),
43:   createdAt: timestamp("createdAt").defaultNow().notNull(),
44:   updatedAt: timestamp("updatedAt").defaultNow().onUpdateNow().notNull(),
45: });
46: export type User = typeof users.$inferSelect;
47: export type InsertUser = typeof users.$inferInsert;
48: export type BusinessInfo = typeof businessInfo.$inferSelect;
49: export type InsertBusinessInfo = typeof businessInfo.$inferInsert;

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/scripts/audit-public-routes.sh
================
 1: set -euo pipefail
 2: base_url="https://3000-iosf6cd1hbktth1n82zss-995aadcb.us2.manus.computer"
 3: report="/home/ubuntu/well-lived-citizen-site/public-route-audit.txt"
 4: cat /dev/null > "$report"
 5: routes=(
 6:   "/"
 7:   "/about"
 8:   "/services"
 9:   "/services/home-organization"
10:   "/services/house-calls"
11:   "/services/legacy"
12:   "/services/resale"
13:   "/pricing"
14:   "/contact"
15: )
16: for route in "${routes[@]}"; do
17:   html="$(curl -L -s "${base_url}${route}")"
18:   {
19:     echo "ROUTE ${route}"
20:     printf '%s\n' "$html" | grep -o '<title>[^<]*</title>' | head -n 1 || true
21:     printf '%s\n' "$html" | grep -Eo 'tel:[0-9]+' | sort -u | tr '\n' ' ' || true
22:     printf '\n'
23:     printf '%s\n' "$html" | grep -Eo 'mailto:[^" >]+' | sort -u | tr '\n' ' ' || true
24:     printf '\n'
25:     printf '%s\n' "$html" | grep -Eo 'https://formspree.io/f/[A-Za-z0-9]+' | sort -u | tr '\n' ' ' || true
26:     printf '\n----\n'
27:   } >> "$report"
28: done
29: cat "$report"

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/scripts/seed-business-info.mjs
================
 1: import fs from "node:fs/promises";
 2: import mysql from "mysql2/promise";
 3: 
 4: const BUSINESS_INFO_ID = 1;
 5: const sourcePath = "/home/ubuntu/wlc_zip_review/skills/well-lived-citizen/references/business-info.json";
 6: 
 7: if (!process.env.DATABASE_URL) {
 8:   throw new Error("DATABASE_URL is required to seed business info.");
 9: }
10: 
11: const raw = await fs.readFile(sourcePath, "utf8");
12: const seed = JSON.parse(raw);
13: 
14: const values = {
15:   id: BUSINESS_INFO_ID,
16:   businessName: seed.businessName || "The Well Lived Citizen",
17:   legalEntity: seed.legalEntity || "Well Dressed Citizen LLC",
18:   city: seed.city || "Los Angeles",
19:   serviceArea: "Los Angeles and surrounding areas.",
20:   primaryPhone: "(323) 433-1350",
21:   primaryPhoneRaw: "3234331350",
22:   workingPhone: "(310) 993-0204",
23:   workingPhoneRaw: "3109930204",
24:   zellePhone: seed.zellePhone || "(310) 993-0204",
25:   zellePhoneRaw: seed.zellePhoneRaw || "3109930204",
26:   primaryEmail: seed.primaryEmail || "dayna@thewelllivedcitizen.com",
27:   zelleEmail: seed.zelleEmail || seed.primaryEmail || "dayna@thewelllivedcitizen.com",
28:   venmoHandle: seed.venmoHandle || "",
29:   stripePaymentLink: seed.stripePaymentLink || "",
30:   calendarLink: seed.calendarLink || "",
31:   instagramMain: seed.instagramMain || "https://instagram.com/thewelllivedcitizen",
32:   instagramCloset: seed.instagramCloset || "https://instagram.com/thewelllivedcloset",
33:   instagramArchive: seed.instagramArchive || "https://instagram.com/welldressedcitizen",
34:   facebook: seed.facebook || "https://facebook.com/thewelllivedcitizen",
35:   poshmarkUrl: seed.poshmarkUrl || "https://posh.mk/HLUmmsrzq2b",
36:   ebayUrl: seed.ebayUrl || "https://ebay.us/m/cUjlUb",
37:   responseTime: seed.responseTime || "Within 24 hours. Text for urgent requests.",
38:   hoursNote: "By appointment. Text for urgent requests.",
39:   paymentNote: "Zelle using the email below.",
40:   homeOrganizationSummary: "Home Organization & Modern Move",
41:   legacySummary: "Legacy Planning & Inventory Catalog",
42:   houseCallsSummary: "House Calls",
43:   resaleSummary: "Curated Resale & Consignment",
44: };
45: 
46: const columns = Object.keys(values);
47: const placeholders = columns.map(() => "?").join(", ");
48: const updateClause = columns
49:   .filter((column) => column !== "id")
50:   .map((column) => `${column} = VALUES(${column})`)
51:   .join(", ");
52: 
53: const sql = `
54:   INSERT INTO businessInfo (${columns.join(", ")})
55:   VALUES (${placeholders})
56:   ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE ${updateClause}
57: `;
58: 
59: const connection = await mysql.createConnection(process.env.DATABASE_URL);
60: 
61: try {
62:   await connection.execute(sql, columns.map((column) => values[column]));
63:   const [rows] = await connection.execute(
64:     "SELECT id, businessName, primaryPhone, primaryPhoneRaw, workingPhone, workingPhoneRaw, primaryEmail, zelleEmail FROM businessInfo WHERE id = ? LIMIT 1",
65:     [BUSINESS_INFO_ID],
66:   );
67:   console.log(JSON.stringify(rows, null, 2));
68: } finally {
69:   await connection.end();
70: }

 4: export type TrpcContext = {
 5:   req: CreateExpressContextOptions["req"];
 6:   res: CreateExpressContextOptions["res"];
 7:   user: User | null;
 8: };
 9: export async function createContext(
10:   opts: CreateExpressContextOptions
11: ): Promise<TrpcContext> {
12:   let user: User | null = null;
13:   try {
14:     user = await sdk.authenticateRequest(opts.req);
15:   } catch (error) {
16:     user = null;

19:     req: opts.req,
20:     res: opts.res,

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/server/_core/cookies.ts

 1: import type { CookieOptions, Request } from "express";
 2: const LOCAL_HOSTS = new Set(["localhost", "127.0.0.1", "::1"]);
 3: function isIpAddress(host: string) {
 4:   if (/^\d{1,3}(\.\d{1,3}){3}$/.test(host)) return true;
 5:   return host.includes(":");
 6: }
 7: function isSecureRequest(req: Request) {
 8:   if (req.protocol === "https") return true;
 9:   const forwardedProto = req.headers["x-forwarded-proto"];
10:   if (!forwardedProto) return false;
11:   const protoList = Array.isArray(forwardedProto)
12:     ? forwardedProto
13:     : forwardedProto.split(",");
14:   return protoList.some(proto => proto.trim().toLowerCase() === "https");
15: }
16: export function getSessionCookieOptions(
17:   req: Request
18: ): Pick<CookieOptions, "domain" | "httpOnly" | "path" | "sameSite" | "secure"> {
19:   return {
20:     httpOnly: true,
21:     path: "/",
22:     sameSite: "none",
23:     secure: isSecureRequest(req),
24:   };
25: }

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/server/_core/dataApi.ts
================
 1: import { ENV } from "./env";
 2: export type DataApiCallOptions = {
 3:   query?: Record<string, unknown>;
 4:   body?: Record<string, unknown>;
 5:   pathParams?: Record<string, unknown>;
 6:   formData?: Record<string, unknown>;
 7: };
 8: export async function callDataApi(
 9:   apiId: string,
10:   options: DataApiCallOptions = {}
11: ): Promise<unknown> {
12:   if (!ENV.forgeApiUrl) {
13:     throw new Error("BUILT_IN_FORGE_API_URL is not configured");
14:   }
15:   if (!ENV.forgeApiKey) {
16:     throw new Error("BUILT_IN_FORGE_API_KEY is not configured");
17:   }
18:   const baseUrl = ENV.forgeApiUrl.endsWith("/") ? ENV.forgeApiUrl : `${ENV.forgeApiUrl}/`;
19:   const fullUrl = new URL("webdevtoken.v1.WebDevService/CallApi", baseUrl).toString();
20:   const response = await fetch(fullUrl, {
21:     method: "POST",
22:     headers: {
23:       accept: "application/json",
24:       "content-type": "application/json",
25:       "connect-protocol-version": "1",
26:       authorization: `Bearer ${ENV.forgeApiKey}`,
27:     },
28:     body: JSON.stringify({
29:       apiId,
30:       query: options.query,
31:       body: options.body,
32:       path_params: options.pathParams,
33:       multipart_form_data: options.formData,
34:     }),
35:   });
36:   if (!response.ok) {
37:     const detail = await response.text().catch(() => "");
38:     throw new Error(
39:       `Data API request failed (${response.status} ${response.statusText})${detail ? `: ${detail}` : ""}`
40:     );
41:   }
42:   const payload = await response.json().catch(() => ({}));
43:   if (payload && typeof payload === "object" && "jsonData" in payload) {
44:     try {
45:       return JSON.parse((payload as Record<string, string>).jsonData ?? "{}");
46:     } catch {
47:       return (payload as Record<string, unknown>).jsonData;
48:     }
49:   }
50:   return payload;
51: }

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/server/_core/imageGeneration.ts
================
 1: import { storagePut } from "server/storage";
 2: import { ENV } from "./env";
 3: export type GenerateImageOptions = {
 4:   prompt: string;
 5:   originalImages?: Array<{
 6:     url?: string;
 7:     b64Json?: string;
 8:     mimeType?: string;
 9:   }>;
10: };
11: export type GenerateImageResponse = {
12:   url?: string;
13: };
14: export async function generateImage(
15:   options: GenerateImageOptions
16: ): Promise<GenerateImageResponse> {
17:   if (!ENV.forgeApiUrl) {
18:     throw new Error("BUILT_IN_FORGE_API_URL is not configured");
19:   }
20:   if (!ENV.forgeApiKey) {
21:     throw new Error("BUILT_IN_FORGE_API_KEY is not configured");
22:   }
23:   const baseUrl = ENV.forgeApiUrl.endsWith("/")
24:     ? ENV.forgeApiUrl
25:     : `${ENV.forgeApiUrl}/`;
26:   const fullUrl = new URL(
27:     "images.v1.ImageService/GenerateImage",
28:     baseUrl
29:   ).toString();
30:   const response = await fetch(fullUrl, {
31:     method: "POST",
32:     headers: {
33:       accept: "application/json",
34:       "content-type": "application/json",
35:       "connect-protocol-version": "1",
36:       authorization: `Bearer ${ENV.forgeApiKey}`,
37:     },
38:     body: JSON.stringify({
39:       prompt: options.prompt,
40:       original_images: options.originalImages || [],
41:     }),
42:   });
43:   if (!response.ok) {
44:     const detail = await response.text().catch(() => "");
45:     throw new Error(
46:       `Image generation request failed (${response.status} ${response.statusText})${detail ? `: ${detail}` : ""}`
47:     );
48:   }
49:   const result = (await response.json()) as {
50:     image: {
51:       b64Json: string;
52:       mimeType: string;
53:     };
54:   };
55:   const base64Data = result.image.b64Json;
56:   const buffer = Buffer.from(base64Data, "base64");
57:   const { url } = await storagePut(
58:     `generated/${Date.now()}.png`,
59:     buffer,
60:     result.image.mimeType
61:   );
62:   return {
63:     url,
64:   };
65: }

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/server/_core/index.ts
================
 1: import "dotenv/config";
 2: import express from "express";
 3: import { createServer } from "http";
 4: import net from "net";
 5: import { createExpressMiddleware } from "@trpc/server/adapters/express";
 6: import { registerOAuthRoutes } from "./oauth";
 7: import { registerStorageProxy } from "./storageProxy";
 8: import { appRouter } from "../routers";
 9: import { createContext } from "./context";
10: import { serveStatic, setupVite } from "./vite";
11: import { getBusinessInfo, upsertBusinessInfo } from "../db";
12: import { registerRecoveredPublicSite } from "../publicSite";
13: function isPortAvailable(port: number): Promise<boolean> {
14:   return new Promise(resolve => {
15:     const server = net.createServer();
16:     server.listen(port, () => {
17:       server.close(() => resolve(true));
18:     });
19:     server.on("error", () => resolve(false));
20:   });
21: }
22: async function findAvailablePort(startPort: number = 3000): Promise<number> {
23:   for (let port = startPort; port < startPort + 20; port++) {
24:     if (await isPortAvailable(port)) {
25:       return port;
26:     }
27:   }
28:   throw new Error(`No available port found starting from ${startPort}`);
29: }
30: async function startServer() {
31:   const app = express();
32:   const server = createServer(app);
33:   app.use(express.json({ limit: "50mb" }));
34:   app.use(express.urlencoded({ limit: "50mb", extended: true }));
35:   registerStorageProxy(app);
36:   registerOAuthRoutes(app);
37:   app.get("/api/business-info", async (_req, res, next) => {
38:     try {
39:       const existing = await getBusinessInfo();
40:       if (existing) {
41:         res.json(existing);
42:         return;
43:       }
44:       await upsertBusinessInfo({});
45:       const fallback = await getBusinessInfo();
46:       res.json(fallback ?? {});
47:     } catch (error) {
48:       next(error);
49:     }
50:   });
51:   registerRecoveredPublicSite(app);
52:   app.use(
53:     "/api/trpc",
54:     createExpressMiddleware({
55:       router: appRouter,
56:       createContext,
57:     })
58:   );
59:   if (process.env.NODE_ENV === "development") {
60:     await setupVite(app, server);
61:   } else {
62:     serveStatic(app);
63:   }
64:   const preferredPort = parseInt(process.env.PORT || "3000");
65:   const port = await findAvailablePort(preferredPort);
66:   if (port !== preferredPort) {
67:     console.log(`Port ${preferredPort} is busy, using port ${port} instead`);
68:   }
69:   server.listen(port, () => {
70:     console.log(`Server running on http://localhost:${port}/`);
71:   });
72: }
73: startServer().catch(console.error);

  1: import { ENV } from "./env";
  2: export type Role = "system" | "user" | "assistant" | "tool" | "function";
  3: export type TextContent = {
  4:   type: "text";
  5:   text: string;
  6: };
  7: export type ImageContent = {
  8:   type: "image_url";
  9:   image_url: {
 10:     url: string;
 11:     detail?: "auto" | "low" | "high";
 12:   };
 13: };
 14: export type FileContent = {
 15:   type: "file_url";
 16:   file_url: {
 17:     url: string;
 18:     mime_type?: "audio/mpeg" | "audio/wav" | "application/pdf" | "audio/mp4" | "video/mp4" ;
 19:   };
 20: };
 21: export type MessageContent = string | TextContent | ImageContent | FileContent;
 22: export type Message = {
 23:   role: Role;
 24:   content: MessageContent | MessageContent[];
 25:   name?: string;
 26:   tool_call_id?: string;
 27: };
 28: export type Tool = {
 29:   type: "function";
 30:   function: {
 31:     name: string;
 32:     description?: string;
 33:     parameters?: Record<string, unknown>;
 34:   };
 35: };
 36: export type ToolChoicePrimitive = "none" | "auto" | "required";
 37: export type ToolChoiceByName = { name: string };
 38: export type ToolChoiceExplicit = {
 39:   type: "function";
 40:   function: {
 41:     name: string;
 42:   };
 43: };
 44: export type ToolChoice =
 45:   | ToolChoicePrimitive
 46:   | ToolChoiceByName
 47:   | ToolChoiceExplicit;
 48: export type InvokeParams = {
 49:   messages: Message[];
 50:   tools?: Tool[];
 51:   toolChoice?: ToolChoice;
 52:   tool_choice?: ToolChoice;
 53:   maxTokens?: number;
 54:   max_tokens?: number;
 55:   outputSchema?: OutputSchema;
 56:   output_schema?: OutputSchema;
 57:   responseFormat?: ResponseFormat;
 58:   response_format?: ResponseFormat;
 59: };
 60: export type ToolCall = {
 61:   id: string;
 62:   type: "function";
 63:   function: {
 64:     name: string;
 65:     arguments: string;
 66:   };
 67: };
 68: export type InvokeResult = {
 69:   id: string;
 70:   created: number;
 71:   model: string;
 72:   choices: Array<{
 73:     index: number;
 74:     message: {
 75:       role: Role;
 76:       content: string | Array<TextContent | ImageContent | FileContent>;
 77:       tool_calls?: ToolCall[];
 78:     };
 79:     finish_reason: string | null;
 80:   }>;
 81:   usage?: {
 82:     prompt_tokens: number;
 83:     completion_tokens: number;
 84:     total_tokens: number;
 85:   };
 86: };
 87: export type JsonSchema = {
 88:   name: string;
 89:   schema: Record<string, unknown>;
 90:   strict?: boolean;
 91: };
 92: export type OutputSchema = JsonSchema;
 93: export type ResponseFormat =
 94:   | { type: "text" }
 95:   | { type: "json_object" }
 96:   | { type: "json_schema"; json_schema: JsonSchema };
 97: const ensureArray = (
 98:   value: MessageContent | MessageContent[]
 99: ): MessageContent[] => (Array.isArray(value) ? value : [value]);
100: const normalizeContentPart = (
101:   part: MessageContent
102: ): TextContent | ImageContent | FileContent => {
103:   if (typeof part === "string") {
104:     return { type: "text", text: part };
105:   }
106:   if (part.type === "text") {
107:     return part;
108:   }
109:   if (part.type === "image_url") {
110:     return part;
111:   }
112:   if (part.type === "file_url") {
113:     return part;
114:   }
115:   throw new Error("Unsupported message content part");
116: };
117: const normalizeMessage = (message: Message) => {
118:   const { role, name, tool_call_id } = message;
119:   if (role === "tool" || role === "function") {
120:     const content = ensureArray(message.content)
121:       .map(part => (typeof part === "string" ? part : JSON.stringify(part)))
122:       .join("\n");
123:     return {
124:       role,
125:       name,
126:       tool_call_id,
127:       content,
128:     };
129:   }
130:   const contentParts = ensureArray(message.content).map(normalizeContentPart);
131:   if (contentParts.length === 1 && contentParts[0].type === "text") {
132:     return {
133:       role,
134:       name,
135:       content: contentParts[0].text,
136:     };
137:   }
138:   return {
139:     role,
140:     name,
141:     content: contentParts,
142:   };
143: };
144: const normalizeToolChoice = (
145:   toolChoice: ToolChoice | undefined,
146:   tools: Tool[] | undefined
147: ): "none" | "auto" | ToolChoiceExplicit | undefined => {
148:   if (!toolChoice) return undefined;
149:   if (toolChoice === "none" || toolChoice === "auto") {
150:     return toolChoice;
151:   }
152:   if (toolChoice === "required") {
153:     if (!tools || tools.length === 0) {
154:       throw new Error(
155:         "tool_choice 'required' was provided but no tools were configured"
156:       );
157:     }
158:     if (tools.length > 1) {
159:       throw new Error(
160:         "tool_choice 'required' needs a single tool or specify the tool name explicitly"
161:       );
162:     }
163:     return {
164:       type: "function",
165:       function: { name: tools[0].function.name },
166:     };
167:   }
168:   if ("name" in toolChoice) {
169:     return {
170:       type: "function",
171:       function: { name: toolChoice.name },
172:     };
173:   }
174:   return toolChoice;
175: };
176: const resolveApiUrl = () =>
177:   ENV.forgeApiUrl && ENV.forgeApiUrl.trim().length > 0
178:     ? `${ENV.forgeApiUrl.replace(/\/$/, "")}/v1/chat/completions`
179:     : "https://forge.manus.im/v1/chat/completions";
180: const assertApiKey = () => {
181:   if (!ENV.forgeApiKey) {
182:     throw new Error("OPENAI_API_KEY is not configured");
183:   }
184: };
185: const normalizeResponseFormat = ({
186:   responseFormat,
187:   response_format,
188:   outputSchema,
189:   output_schema,
190: }: {
191:   responseFormat?: ResponseFormat;
192:   response_format?: ResponseFormat;
193:   outputSchema?: OutputSchema;
194:   output_schema?: OutputSchema;
195: }):
196:   | { type: "json_schema"; json_schema: JsonSchema }
197:   | { type: "text" }
198:   | { type: "json_object" }
199:   | undefined => {
200:   const explicitFormat = responseFormat || response_format;
201:   if (explicitFormat) {
202:     if (
203:       explicitFormat.type === "json_schema" &&
204:       !explicitFormat.json_schema?.schema
205:     ) {
206:       throw new Error(
207:         "responseFormat json_schema requires a defined schema object"
208:       );
209:     }
210:     return explicitFormat;
211:   }
212:   const schema = outputSchema || output_schema;
213:   if (!schema) return undefined;
214:   if (!schema.name || !schema.schema) {
215:     throw new Error("outputSchema requires both name and schema");
216:   }
217:   return {
218:     type: "json_schema",
219:     json_schema: {
220:       name: schema.name,
221:       schema: schema.schema,
222:       ...(typeof schema.strict === "boolean" ? { strict: schema.strict } : {}),
223:     },
224:   };
225: };
226: export async function invokeLLM(params: InvokeParams): Promise<InvokeResult> {
227:   assertApiKey();
228:   const {
229:     messages,
230:     tools,
231:     toolChoice,
232:     tool_choice,
233:     outputSchema,
234:     output_schema,
235:     responseFormat,
236:     response_format,
237:   } = params;
238:   const payload: Record<string, unknown> = {
239:     model: "gemini-2.5-flash",
240:     messages: messages.map(normalizeMessage),
241:   };
242:   if (tools && tools.length > 0) {
243:     payload.tools = tools;
244:   }
245:   const normalizedToolChoice = normalizeToolChoice(
246:     toolChoice || tool_choice,
247:     tools
248:   );
249:   if (normalizedToolChoice) {
250:     payload.tool_choice = normalizedToolChoice;
251:   }
252:   payload.max_tokens = 32768
253:   payload.thinking = {
254:     "budget_tokens": 128
255:   }
256:   const normalizedResponseFormat = normalizeResponseFormat({
257:     responseFormat,
258:     response_format,
259:     outputSchema,
260:     output_schema,
261:   });
262:   if (normalizedResponseFormat) {
263:     payload.response_format = normalizedResponseFormat;
264:   }
265:   const response = await fetch(resolveApiUrl(), {
266:     method: "POST",
267:     headers: {
268:       "content-type": "application/json",
269:       authorization: `Bearer ${ENV.forgeApiKey}`,
270:     },
271:     body: JSON.stringify(payload),
272:   });
273:   if (!response.ok) {
274:     const errorText = await response.text();
275:     throw new Error(
276:       `LLM invoke failed: ${response.status} ${response.statusText} – ${errorText}`
277:     );
278:   }
279:   return (await response.json()) as InvokeResult;
280: }

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/server/_core/map.ts

  1: import { ENV } from "./env";
  2: type MapsConfig = {
  3:   baseUrl: string;
  4:   apiKey: string;
  5: };
  6: function getMapsConfig(): MapsConfig {
  7:   const baseUrl = ENV.forgeApiUrl;
  8:   const apiKey = ENV.forgeApiKey;
  9:   if (!baseUrl || !apiKey) {
 10:     throw new Error(
 11:       "Google Maps proxy credentials missing: set BUILT_IN_FORGE_API_URL and BUILT_IN_FORGE_API_KEY"
 12:     );
 13:   }
 14:   return {
 15:     baseUrl: baseUrl.replace(/\/+$/, ""),
 16:     apiKey,
 17:   };
 18: }
 19: // ============================================================================
 20: // Core Request Handler
 21: // ============================================================================
 22: interface RequestOptions {
 23:   method?: "GET" | "POST";
 24:   body?: Record<string, unknown>;
 25: }
 26: export async function makeRequest<T = unknown>(
 27:   endpoint: string,
 28:   params: Record<string, unknown> = {},
 29:   options: RequestOptions = {}
 30: ): Promise<T> {
 31:   const { baseUrl, apiKey } = getMapsConfig();
 32:   const url = new URL(`${baseUrl}/v1/maps/proxy${endpoint}`);
 33:   url.searchParams.append("key", apiKey);
 34:   Object.entries(params).forEach(([key, value]) => {
 35:     if (value !== undefined && value !== null) {
 36:       url.searchParams.append(key, String(value));
 37:     }
 38:   });
 39:   const response = await fetch(url.toString(), {
 40:     method: options.method || "GET",
 41:     headers: {
 42:       "Content-Type": "application/json",
 43:     },
 44:     body: options.body ? JSON.stringify(options.body) : undefined,
 45:   });
 46:   if (!response.ok) {
 47:     const errorText = await response.text();
 48:     throw new Error(
 49:       `Google Maps API request failed (${response.status} ${response.statusText}): ${errorText}`
 50:     );
 51:   }
 52:   return (await response.json()) as T;
 53: }

================
File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/server/_core/notification.ts
================
 1: import { TRPCError } from "@trpc/server";
 2: import { ENV } from "./env";
 3: export type NotificationPayload = {
 4:   title: string;
 5:   content: string;
 6: };
 7: const TITLE_MAX_LENGTH = 1200;
 8: const CONTENT_MAX_LENGTH = 20000;
 9: const trimValue = (value: string): string => value.trim();
10: const isNonEmptyString = (value: unknown): value is string =>
11:   typeof value === "string" && value.trim().length > 0;
12: const buildEndpointUrl = (baseUrl: string): string => {
13:   const normalizedBase = baseUrl.endsWith("/")
14:     ? baseUrl
15:     : `${baseUrl}/`;
16:   return new URL(
17:     "webdevtoken.v1.WebDevService/SendNotification",
18:     normalizedBase
19:   ).toString();
20: };
21: const validatePayload = (input: NotificationPayload): NotificationPayload => {
22:   if (!isNonEmptyString(input.title)) {
23:     throw new TRPCError({
24:       code: "BAD_REQUEST",
25:       message: "Notification title is required.",
26:     });
27:   }
28:   if (!isNonEmptyString(input.content)) {
29:     throw new TRPCError({
30:       code: "BAD_REQUEST",
31:       message: "Notification content is required.",
32:     });
33:   }
34:   const title = trimValue(input.title);
35:   const content = trimValue(input.content);
36:   if (title.length > TITLE_MAX_LENGTH) {
37:     throw new TRPCError({
38:       code: "BAD_REQUEST",
39:       message: `Notification title must be at most ${TITLE_MAX_LENGTH} characters.`,
40:     });
41:   }
42:   if (content.length > CONTENT_MAX_LENGTH) {
43:     throw new TRPCError({
44:       code: "BAD_REQUEST",
45:       message: `Notification content must be at most ${CONTENT_MAX_LENGTH} characters.`,
46:     });
47:   }
48:   return { title, content };
49: };
50: export async function notifyOwner(
51:   payload: NotificationPayload
52: ): Promise<boolean> {
53:   const { title, content } = validatePayload(payload);
54:   if (!ENV.forgeApiUrl) {
55:     throw new TRPCError({
56:       code: "INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR",
57:       message: "Notification service URL is not configured.",
58:     });
59:   }
60:   if (!ENV.forgeApiKey) {
61:     throw new TRPCError({
62:       code: "INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR",
63:       message: "Notification service API key is not configured.",
64:     });
65:   }
66:   const endpoint = buildEndpointUrl(ENV.forgeApiUrl);
67:   try {
68:     const response = await fetch(endpoint, {
69:       method: "POST",
70:       headers: {
71:         accept: "application/json",
72:         authorization: `Bearer ${ENV.forgeApiKey}`,
73:         "content-type": "application/json",
74:         "connect-protocol-version": "1",
75:       },
76:       body: JSON.stringify({ title, content }),
77:     });
78:     if (!response.ok) {
79:       const detail = await response.text().catch(() => "");
80:       console.warn(
81:         `[Notification] Failed to notify owner (${response.status} ${response.statusText})${
82:           detail ? `: ${detail}` : ""
83:         }`
84:       );
85:       return false;
86:     }
87:     return true;
88:   } catch (error) {
89:     console.warn("[Notification] Error calling notification service:", error);
90:     return false;
91:   }
92: }

================
File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/server/_core/oauth.ts
================
 1: import { COOKIE_NAME, ONE_YEAR_MS } from "@shared/const";
 2: import type { Express, Request, Response } from "express";
 3: import * as db from "../db";
 4: import { getSessionCookieOptions } from "./cookies";
 5: import { sdk } from "./sdk";
 6: function getQueryParam(req: Request, key: string): string | undefined {
 7:   const value = req.query[key];
 8:   return typeof value === "string" ? value : undefined;
 9: }
10: export function registerOAuthRoutes(app: Express) {
11:   app.get("/api/oauth/callback", async (req: Request, res: Response) => {
12:     const code = getQueryParam(req, "code");
13:     const state = getQueryParam(req, "state");
14:     if (!code || !state) {
15:       res.status(400).json({ error: "code and state are required" });
16:       return;
17:     }
18:     try {
19:       const tokenResponse = await sdk.exchangeCodeForToken(code, state);
20:       const userInfo = await sdk.getUserInfo(tokenResponse.accessToken);
21:       if (!userInfo.openId) {
22:         res.status(400).json({ error: "openId missing from user info" });
23:         return;
24:       }
25:       await db.upsertUser({
26:         openId: userInfo.openId,
27:         name: userInfo.name || null,
28:         email: userInfo.email ?? null,
29:         loginMethod: userInfo.loginMethod ?? userInfo.platform ?? null,
30:         lastSignedIn: new Date(),
31:       });
32:       const sessionToken = await sdk.createSessionToken(userInfo.openId, {
33:         name: userInfo.name || "",
34:         expiresInMs: ONE_YEAR_MS,
35:       });
36:       const cookieOptions = getSessionCookieOptions(req);
37:       res.cookie(COOKIE_NAME, sessionToken, { ...cookieOptions, maxAge: ONE_YEAR_MS });
38:       res.redirect(302, "/");
39:     } catch (error) {
40:       console.error("[OAuth] Callback failed", error);
41:       res.status(500).json({ error: "OAuth callback failed" });
42:     }
43:   });
44: }

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/server/_core/sdk.ts
================
  1: import { AXIOS_TIMEOUT_MS, COOKIE_NAME, ONE_YEAR_MS } from "@shared/const";
  2: import { ForbiddenError } from "@shared/_core/errors";
  3: import axios, { type AxiosInstance } from "axios";
  4: import { parse as parseCookieHeader } from "cookie";
  5: import type { Request } from "express";
  6: import { SignJWT, jwtVerify } from "jose";
  7: import type { User } from "../../drizzle/schema";
  8: import * as db from "../db";
  9: import { ENV } from "./env";
 10: import type {
 11:   ExchangeTokenRequest,
 12:   ExchangeTokenResponse,
 13:   GetUserInfoResponse,
 14:   GetUserInfoWithJwtRequest,
 15:   GetUserInfoWithJwtResponse,
 16: } from "./types/manusTypes";
 17: const isNonEmptyString = (value: unknown): value is string =>
 18:   typeof value === "string" && value.length > 0;
 19: export type SessionPayload = {
 20:   openId: string;
 21:   appId: string;
 22:   name: string;
 23: };
 24: const EXCHANGE_TOKEN_PATH = `/webdev.v1.WebDevAuthPublicService/ExchangeToken`;
 25: const GET_USER_INFO_PATH = `/webdev.v1.WebDevAuthPublicService/GetUserInfo`;
 26: const GET_USER_INFO_WITH_JWT_PATH = `/webdev.v1.WebDevAuthPublicService/GetUserInfoWithJwt`;
 27: class OAuthService {
 28:   constructor(private client: ReturnType<typeof axios.create>) {
 29:     console.log("[OAuth] Initialized with baseURL:", ENV.oAuthServerUrl);
 30:     if (!ENV.oAuthServerUrl) {
 31:       console.error(
 32:         "[OAuth] ERROR: OAUTH_SERVER_URL is not configured! Set OAUTH_SERVER_URL environment variable."
 33:       );
 34:     }
 35:   }
 36:   private decodeState(state: string): string {
 37:     const redirectUri = atob(state);
 38:     return redirectUri;
 39:   }
 40:   async getTokenByCode(
 41:     code: string,
 42:     state: string
 43:   ): Promise<ExchangeTokenResponse> {
 44:     const payload: ExchangeTokenRequest = {
 45:       clientId: ENV.appId,
 46:       grantType: "authorization_code",
 47:       code,
 48:       redirectUri: this.decodeState(state),
 49:     };
 50:     const { data } = await this.client.post<ExchangeTokenResponse>(
 51:       EXCHANGE_TOKEN_PATH,
 52:       payload
 53:     );
 54:     return data;
 55:   }
 56:   async getUserInfoByToken(
 57:     token: ExchangeTokenResponse
 58:   ): Promise<GetUserInfoResponse> {
 59:     const { data } = await this.client.post<GetUserInfoResponse>(
 60:       GET_USER_INFO_PATH,
 61:       {
 62:         accessToken: token.accessToken,
 63:       }
 64:     );
 65:     return data;
 66:   }
 67: }
 68: const createOAuthHttpClient = (): AxiosInstance =>
 69:   axios.create({
 70:     baseURL: ENV.oAuthServerUrl,
 71:     timeout: AXIOS_TIMEOUT_MS,
 72:   });
 73: class SDKServer {
 74:   private readonly client: AxiosInstance;
 75:   private readonly oauthService: OAuthService;
 76:   constructor(client: AxiosInstance = createOAuthHttpClient()) {
 77:     this.client = client;
 78:     this.oauthService = new OAuthService(this.client);
 79:   }
 80:   private deriveLoginMethod(
 81:     platforms: unknown,
 82:     fallback: string | null | undefined
 83:   ): string | null {
 84:     if (fallback && fallback.length > 0) return fallback;
 85:     if (!Array.isArray(platforms) || platforms.length === 0) return null;
 86:     const set = new Set<string>(
 87:       platforms.filter((p): p is string => typeof p === "string")
 88:     );
 89:     if (set.has("REGISTERED_PLATFORM_EMAIL")) return "email";
 90:     if (set.has("REGISTERED_PLATFORM_GOOGLE")) return "google";
 91:     if (set.has("REGISTERED_PLATFORM_APPLE")) return "apple";
 92:     if (
 93:       set.has("REGISTERED_PLATFORM_MICROSOFT") ||
 94:       set.has("REGISTERED_PLATFORM_AZURE")
 95:     )
 96:       return "microsoft";
 97:     if (set.has("REGISTERED_PLATFORM_GITHUB")) return "github";
 98:     const first = Array.from(set)[0];
 99:     return first ? first.toLowerCase() : null;
100:   }
101:   async exchangeCodeForToken(
102:     code: string,
103:     state: string
104:   ): Promise<ExchangeTokenResponse> {
105:     return this.oauthService.getTokenByCode(code, state);
106:   }
107:   async getUserInfo(accessToken: string): Promise<GetUserInfoResponse> {
108:     const data = await this.oauthService.getUserInfoByToken({
109:       accessToken,
110:     } as ExchangeTokenResponse);
111:     const loginMethod = this.deriveLoginMethod(
112:       (data as any)?.platforms,
113:       (data as any)?.platform ?? data.platform ?? null
114:     );
115:     return {
116:       ...(data as any),
117:       platform: loginMethod,
118:       loginMethod,
119:     } as GetUserInfoResponse;
120:   }
121:   private parseCookies(cookieHeader: string | undefined) {
122:     if (!cookieHeader) {
123:       return new Map<string, string>();
124:     }
125:     const parsed = parseCookieHeader(cookieHeader);
126:     return new Map(Object.entries(parsed));
127:   }
128:   private getSessionSecret() {
129:     const secret = ENV.cookieSecret;
130:     return new TextEncoder().encode(secret);
131:   }
132:   async createSessionToken(
133:     openId: string,
134:     options: { expiresInMs?: number; name?: string } = {}
135:   ): Promise<string> {
136:     return this.signSession(
137:       {
138:         openId,
139:         appId: ENV.appId,
140:         name: options.name || "",
141:       },
142:       options
143:     );
144:   }
145:   async signSession(
146:     payload: SessionPayload,
147:     options: { expiresInMs?: number } = {}
148:   ): Promise<string> {
149:     const issuedAt = Date.now();
150:     const expiresInMs = options.expiresInMs ?? ONE_YEAR_MS;
151:     const expirationSeconds = Math.floor((issuedAt + expiresInMs) / 1000);
152:     const secretKey = this.getSessionSecret();
153:     return new SignJWT({
154:       openId: payload.openId,
155:       appId: payload.appId,
156:       name: payload.name,
157:     })
158:       .setProtectedHeader({ alg: "HS256", typ: "JWT" })
159:       .setExpirationTime(expirationSeconds)
160:       .sign(secretKey);
161:   }
162:   async verifySession(
163:     cookieValue: string | undefined | null
164:   ): Promise<{ openId: string; appId: string; name: string } | null> {
165:     if (!cookieValue) {
166:       console.warn("[Auth] Missing session cookie");
167:       return null;
168:     }
169:     try {
170:       const secretKey = this.getSessionSecret();
171:       const { payload } = await jwtVerify(cookieValue, secretKey, {
172:         algorithms: ["HS256"],
173:       });
174:       const { openId, appId, name } = payload as Record<string, unknown>;
175:       if (
176:         !isNonEmptyString(openId) ||
177:         !isNonEmptyString(appId) ||
178:         !isNonEmptyString(name)
179:       ) {
180:         console.warn("[Auth] Session payload missing required fields");
181:         return null;
182:       }
183:       return {
184:         openId,
185:         appId,
186:         name,
187:       };
188:     } catch (error) {
189:       console.warn("[Auth] Session verification failed", String(error));
190:       return null;
191:     }
192:   }
193:   async getUserInfoWithJwt(
194:     jwtToken: string
195:   ): Promise<GetUserInfoWithJwtResponse> {
196:     const payload: GetUserInfoWithJwtRequest = {
197:       jwtToken,
198:       projectId: ENV.appId,
199:     };
200:     const { data } = await this.client.post<GetUserInfoWithJwtResponse>(
201:       GET_USER_INFO_WITH_JWT_PATH,
202:       payload
203:     );
204:     const loginMethod = this.deriveLoginMethod(
205:       (data as any)?.platforms,
206:       (data as any)?.platform ?? data.platform ?? null
207:     );
208:     return {
209:       ...(data as any),
210:       platform: loginMethod,
211:       loginMethod,
212:     } as GetUserInfoWithJwtResponse;
213:   }
214:   async authenticateRequest(req: Request): Promise<User> {
215:     const cookies = this.parseCookies(req.headers.cookie);
216:     const sessionCookie = cookies.get(COOKIE_NAME);
217:     const session = await this.verifySession(sessionCookie);
218:     if (!session) {
219:       throw ForbiddenError("Invalid session cookie");
220:     }
221:     const sessionUserId = session.openId;
222:     const signedInAt = new Date();
223:     let user = await db.getUserByOpenId(sessionUserId);
224:     if (!user) {
225:       try {
226:         const userInfo = await this.getUserInfoWithJwt(sessionCookie ?? "");
227:         await db.upsertUser({
228:           openId: userInfo.openId,
229:           name: userInfo.name || null,
230:           email: userInfo.email ?? null,
231:           loginMethod: userInfo.loginMethod ?? userInfo.platform ?? null,
232:           lastSignedIn: signedInAt,
233:         });
234:         user = await db.getUserByOpenId(userInfo.openId);
235:       } catch (error) {
236:         console.error("[Auth] Failed to sync user from OAuth:", error);
237:         throw ForbiddenError("Failed to sync user info");
238:       }
239:     }
240:     if (!user) {
241:       throw ForbiddenError("User not found");
242:     }
243:     await db.upsertUser({
244:       openId: user.openId,
245:       lastSignedIn: signedInAt,
246:     });
247:     return user;
248:   }
249: }
250: export const sdk = new SDKServer();

================
File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/server/_core/storageProxy.ts
================
 1: import type { Express } from "express";
 2: import { ENV } from "./env";
 3: export function registerStorageProxy(app: Express) {
 4:   app.get("/manus-storage/*", async (req, res) => {
 5:     const key = (req.params as Record<string, string | undefined> & { 0?: string })[0];
 6:     if (!key) {
 7:       res.status(400).send("Missing storage key");
 8:       return;
 9:     }
10:     if (!ENV.forgeApiUrl || !ENV.forgeApiKey) {
11:       res.status(500).send("Storage proxy not configured");
12:       return;
13:     }
14:     try {
15:       const forgeUrl = new URL(
16:         "v1/storage/presign/get",
17:         ENV.forgeApiUrl.replace(/\/+$/, "") + "/",
18:       );
19:       forgeUrl.searchParams.set("path", key);
20:       const forgeResp = await fetch(forgeUrl, {
21:         headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${ENV.forgeApiKey}` },
22:       });
23:       if (!forgeResp.ok) {
24:         const body = await forgeResp.text().catch(() => "");
25:         console.error(`[StorageProxy] forge error: ${forgeResp.status} ${body}`);
26:         res.status(502).send("Storage backend error");
27:         return;
28:       }
29:       const { url } = (await forgeResp.json()) as { url: string };
30:       if (!url) {
31:         res.status(502).send("Empty signed URL from backend");
32:         return;
33:       }
34:       res.set("Cache-Control", "no-store");
35:       res.redirect(307, url);
36:     } catch (err) {
37:       console.error("[StorageProxy] failed:", err);
38:       res.status(502).send("Storage proxy error");
39:     }
40:   });
41: }

 1: import { NOT_ADMIN_ERR_MSG, UNAUTHED_ERR_MSG } from '@shared/const';
 2: import { initTRPC, TRPCError } from "@trpc/server";
 3: import superjson from "superjson";
 4: import type { TrpcContext } from "./context";
 5: const t = initTRPC.context<TrpcContext>().create({
 6:   transformer: superjson,
 7: });
 8: export const router = t.router;
 9: export const publicProcedure = t.procedure;
10: const requireUser = t.middleware(async opts => {
11:   const { ctx, next } = opts;
12:   if (!ctx.user) {
13:     throw new TRPCError({ code: "UNAUTHORIZED", message: UNAUTHED_ERR_MSG });
14:   }
15:   return next({
16:     ctx: {
17:       ...ctx,
18:       user: ctx.user,
19:     },
20:   });
21: });
22: export const protectedProcedure = t.procedure.use(requireUser);
23: export const adminProcedure = t.procedure.use(
24:   t.middleware(async opts => {
25:     const { ctx, next } = opts;
26:     if (!ctx.user || ctx.user.role !== 'admin') {
27:       throw new TRPCError({ code: "FORBIDDEN", message: NOT_ADMIN_ERR_MSG });
28:     }
29:     return next({
30:       ctx: {
31:         ...ctx,
32:         user: ctx.user,
33:       },
34:     });
35:   }),
36: );

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/server/_core/vite.ts
================
 1: import express, { type Express } from "express";
 2: import fs from "fs";
 3: import { type Server } from "http";
 4: import { nanoid } from "nanoid";
 5: import path from "path";
 6: import { createServer as createViteServer } from "vite";
 7: import viteConfig from "../../vite.config";
 8: export async function setupVite(app: Express, server: Server) {
 9:   const serverOptions = {
10:     middlewareMode: true,
11:     hmr: { server },
12:     allowedHosts: true as const,
13:   };
14:   const vite = await createViteServer({
15:     ...viteConfig,
16:     configFile: false,
17:     server: serverOptions,
18:     appType: "custom",
19:   });
20:   app.use(vite.middlewares);
21:   app.use("*", async (req, res, next) => {
22:     const url = req.originalUrl;
23:     try {
24:       const clientTemplate = path.resolve(
25:         import.meta.dirname,
26:         "../..",
27:         "client",
28:         "index.html"
29:       );
30:       let template = await fs.promises.readFile(clientTemplate, "utf-8");
31:       template = template.replace(
32:         `src="/src/main.tsx"`,
33:         `src="/src/main.tsx?v=${nanoid()}"`
34:       );
35:       const page = await vite.transformIndexHtml(url, template);
36:       res.status(200).set({ "Content-Type": "text/html" }).end(page);
37:     } catch (e) {
38:       vite.ssrFixStacktrace(e as Error);
39:       next(e);
40:     }
41:   });
42: }
43: export function serveStatic(app: Express) {
44:   const distPath =
45:     process.env.NODE_ENV === "development"
46:       ? path.resolve(import.meta.dirname, "../..", "dist", "public")
47:       : path.resolve(import.meta.dirname, "public");
48:   if (!fs.existsSync(distPath)) {
49:     console.error(
50:       `Could not find the build directory: ${distPath}, make sure to build the client first`
51:     );
52:   }
53:   app.use(express.static(distPath));
54:   app.use("*", (_req, res) => {
55:     res.sendFile(path.resolve(distPath, "index.html"));
56:   });
57: }

File: well-lived-citizen-site-Claude/server/_core/voiceTranscription.ts

  1: import { ENV } from "./env";
  2: export type TranscribeOptions = {
  3:   audioUrl: string;
  4:   language?: string;
  5:   prompt?: string;
  6: };
  7: export type WhisperSegment = {
  8:   id: number;
  9:   seek: number;
 10:   start: number;
 11:   end: number;
 12:   text: string;
 13:   tokens: number[];
 14:   temperature: number;
 15:   avg_logprob: number;
 16:   compression_ratio: number;
 17:   no_speech_prob: number;
 18: };
 19: export type WhisperResponse = {
 20:   task: "transcribe";
 21:   language: string;
 22:   duration: number;
 23:   text: string;
 24:   segments: WhisperSegment[];
 25: };
 26: export type TranscriptionResponse = WhisperResponse;
 27: export type TranscriptionError = {
 28:   error: string;
 29:   code: "FILE_TOO_LARGE" | "INVALID_FORMAT" | "TRANSCRIPTION_FAILED" | "UPLOAD_FAILED" | "SERVICE_ERROR";
 30:   details?: string;
 31: };
 32: export async function transcribeAudio(
 33:   options: TranscribeOptions
 34: ): Promise<TranscriptionResponse | TranscriptionError> {
 35:   try {
 36:     if (!ENV.forgeApiUrl) {
 37:       return {
 38:         error: "Voice transcription service is not configured",
 39:         code: "SERVICE_ERROR",
 40:         details: "BUILT_IN_FORGE_API_URL is not set"
 41:       };
 42:     }
 43:     if (!ENV.forgeApiKey) {
 44:       return {
 45:         error: "Voice transcription service authentication is missing",
 46:         code: "SERVICE_ERROR",
 47:         details: "BUILT_IN_FORGE_API_KEY is not set"
 48:       };
 49:     }
 50:     let audioBuffer: Buffer;
 51:     let mimeType: string;
 52:     try {
 53:       const response = await fetch(options.audioUrl);
 54:       if (!response.ok) {
 55:         return {
 56:           error: "Failed to download audio file",
 57:           code: "INVALID_FORMAT",
 58:           details: `HTTP ${response.status}: ${response.statusText}`
 59:         };
 60:       }
 61:       audioBuffer = Buffer.from(await response.arrayBuffer());
 62:       mimeType = response.headers.get('content-type') || 'audio/mpeg';
 63:       const sizeMB = audioBuffer.length / (1024 * 1024);
 64:       if (sizeMB > 16) {
 65:         return {
 66:           error: "Audio file exceeds maximum size limit",
 67:           code: "FILE_TOO_LARGE",
 68:           details: `File size is ${sizeMB.toFixed(2)}MB, maximum allowed is 16MB`
 69:         };
 70:       }
 71:     } catch (error) {
 72:       return {
 73:         error: "Failed to fetch audio file",
 74:         code: "SERVICE_ERROR",
 75:         details: error instanceof Error ? error.message : "Unknown error"
 76:       };
 77:     }
 78:     const formData = new FormData();
 79:     const filename = `audio.${getFileExtension(mimeType)}`;
 80:     const audioBlob = new Blob([new Uint8Array(audioBuffer)], { type: mimeType });
 81:     formData.append("file", audioBlob, filename);
 82:     formData.append("model", "whisper-1");
 83:     formData.append("response_format", "verbose_json");
 84:     const prompt = options.prompt || (
 85:       options.language
 86:         ? `Transcribe the user's voice to text, the user's working language is ${getLanguageName(options.language)}`
 87:         : "Transcribe the user's voice to text"
 88:     );
 89:     formData.append("prompt", prompt);
 90:     const baseUrl = ENV.forgeApiUrl.endsWith("/")
 91:       ? ENV.forgeApiUrl
 92:       : `${ENV.forgeApiUrl}/`;
 93:     const fullUrl = new URL(
 94:       "v1/audio/transcriptions",
 95:       baseUrl
 96:     ).toString();
 97:     const response = await fetch(fullUrl, {
 98:       method: "POST",
 99:       headers: {
100:         authorization: `Bearer ${ENV.forgeApiKey}`,
101:         "Accept-Encoding": "identity",
102:       },
103:       body: formData,
104:     });
105:     if (!response.ok) {
106:       const errorText = await response.text().catch(() => "");
107:       return {
108:         error: "Transcription service request failed",
109:         code: "TRANSCRIPTION_FAILED",
110:         details: `${response.status} ${response.statusText}${errorText ? `: ${errorText}` : ""}`
111:       };
112:     }
113:     const whisperResponse = await response.json() as WhisperResponse;
114:     if (!whisperResponse.text || typeof whisperResponse.text !== 'string') {
115:       return {
116:         error: "Invalid transcription response",
117:         code: "SERVICE_ERROR",
118:         details: "Transcription service returned an invalid response format"
119:       };
120:     }
121:     return whisperResponse;
122:   } catch (error) {
123:     return {
124:       error: "Voice transcription failed",
125:       code: "SERVICE_ERROR",
126:       details: error instanceof Error ? error.message : "An unexpected error occurred"
127:     };
128:   }
129: }
130: function getFileExtension(mimeType: string): string {
131:   const mimeToExt: Record<string, string> = {
132:     'audio/webm': 'webm',
133:     'audio/mp3': 'mp3',
134:     'audio/mpeg': 'mp3',
135:     'audio/wav': 'wav',
136:     'audio/wave': 'wav',
137:     'audio/ogg': 'ogg',
138:     'audio/m4a': 'm4a',
139:     'audio/mp4': 'm4a',
140:   };
141:   return mimeToExt[mimeType] || 'audio';
142: }
143: function getLanguageName(langCode: string): string {
144:   const langMap: Record<string, string> = {
145:     'en': 'English',
146:     'es': 'Spanish',
147:     'fr': 'French',
148:     'de': 'German',
149:     'it': 'Italian',
150:     'pt': 'Portuguese',
151:     'ru': 'Russian',
152:     'ja': 'Japanese',
153:     'ko': 'Korean',
154:     'zh': 'Chinese',
155:     'ar': 'Arabic',
156:     'hi': 'Hindi',
157:     'nl': 'Dutch',
158:     'pl': 'Polish',
159:     'tr': 'Turkish',
160:     'sv': 'Swedish',
161:     'da': 'Danish',
162:     'no': 'Norwegian',
163:     'fi': 'Finnish',
164:   };
165:   return langMap[langCode] || langCode;
166: }

 1: import { describe, expect, it } from "vitest";
 2: import { appRouter } from "./routers";
 3: import { COOKIE_NAME } from "../shared/const";
 4: import type { TrpcContext } from "./_core/context";
 5: type CookieCall = {
 6:   name: string;
 7:   options: Record<string, unknown>;
 8: };
 9: type AuthenticatedUser = NonNullable<TrpcContext["user"]>;
10: function createAuthContext(): { ctx: TrpcContext; clearedCookies: CookieCall[] } {
11:   const clearedCookies: CookieCall[] = [];
12:   const user: AuthenticatedUser = {
13:     id: 1,
14:     openId: "sample-user",
15:     email: "sample@example.com",
16:     name: "Sample User",
17:     loginMethod: "manus",
18:     role: "user",
19:     createdAt: new Date(),
20:     updatedAt: new Date(),
21:     lastSignedIn: new Date(),
22:   };
23:   const ctx: TrpcContext = {
24:     user,
25:     req: {
26:       protocol: "https",
27:       headers: {},
28:     } as TrpcContext["req"],
29:     res: {
30:       clearCookie: (name: string, options: Record<string, unknown>) => {
31:         clearedCookies.push({ name, options });
32:       },
33:     } as TrpcContext["res"],
34:   };
35:   return { ctx, clearedCookies };
36: }
37: describe("auth.logout", () => {
38:   it("clears the session cookie and reports success", async () => {
39:     const { ctx, clearedCookies } = createAuthContext();
40:     const caller = appRouter.createCaller(ctx);
41:     const result = await caller.auth.logout();
42:     expect(result).toEqual({ success: true });
43:     expect(clearedCookies).toHaveLength(1);
44:     expect(clearedCookies[0]?.name).toBe(COOKIE_NAME);
45:     expect(clearedCookies[0]?.options).toMatchObject({
46:       maxAge: -1,
47:       secure: true,
48:       sameSite: "none",
49:       httpOnly: true,
50:       path: "/",
51:     });
52:   });
53: });

  1: import { eq } from "drizzle-orm";
  2: import { drizzle } from "drizzle-orm/mysql2";
  3: import { businessInfo, BusinessInfo, InsertBusinessInfo, InsertUser, users } from "../drizzle/schema";
  4: import { ENV } from "./_core/env";
  5: let _db: ReturnType<typeof drizzle> | null = null;
  6: export const BUSINESS_INFO_ID = 1;
  7: const defaultBusinessInfoValues: Omit<InsertBusinessInfo, "id" | "createdAt" | "updatedAt"> = {
  8:   businessName: "The Well Lived Citizen",
  9:   legalEntity: "Well Dressed Citizen LLC",
 10:   city: "Los Angeles",
 11:   serviceArea: "Los Angeles and surrounding areas.",
 12:   primaryPhone: "(323) 433-1350",
 13:   primaryPhoneRaw: "3234331350",
 14:   workingPhone: "(310) 993-0204",
 15:   workingPhoneRaw: "3109930204",
 16:   zellePhone: "(310) 993-0204",
 17:   zellePhoneRaw: "3109930204",
 18:   primaryEmail: "dayna@thewelllivedcitizen.com",
 19:   zelleEmail: "dayna@thewelllivedcitizen.com",
 20:   venmoHandle: "",
 21:   stripePaymentLink: "",
 22:   calendarLink: "",

 25:   instagramArchive: "https://instagram.com/welldressedcitizen",
